國民政府八日令　導淮委員會委員長蔣中正呈請任命朗品元顧世楫胡振亭爲導淮委員會秘書處科長、應照准、此令、

國内要電

英庚欵董事會 2

昨日宣告成立

賀耐當選副董事長

抽籤决定董事任期

（南京）　管理英國退還庚欵董事會、八日晨正式宣告成立、並於上午十時、在鐵部會議廳、開第一次大會、出席者中國方面、朱家驊·陳其采·李書華·程振鈞·葉恭綽·王家楨·黄漢樑·宋子良·曾鎔甫·英國方面賀萊卜隆·端納等十二人、首由朱董事長報告、該會係奉國府之命設立、處理英退還之庚欵、並報告積存與未到期兩部份數目及用途後、因議案甚多、至一時半尙未完事、乃暫時休息、由朱董事長請各董事、在國聯社午餐、下午四時、繼續會議、至六時半閉會、旋接開常務董事會第一次會議、並推定副董事長曁秘書·會計、及王家楨起草會議規則辦事細則、其開會情形如次、（一）用抽籤法抽定董事之任期如下、計一年者、王家楨·宋子良·賀萊·馬錫爾·陳其采、二年者李書華·康德利·葉恭綽·程振鈞·曾鎔甫·三年者端納·曾養甫·卜隆·黄漢樑朱家驊·（二）推選賀萊爲副董事長、黄漢樑爲秘書、曾鎔甫爲會計、（三）討論事項（甲）通過本會應設常務董事會（一）决定常務董事額數爲七人、（二）决定董事長、副董事長、秘書·會計四人、爲當然常務董事、並推舉葉恭綽·王家楨·卜隆三人、爲常務董事、（乙）購料委員會委員人選、照協定換文之規定委員六人、除中國駐英外交代表、及鐵道部代表外、其餘四人、由英政府推荐六人、再由中國政府擇定四人爲委員、當經通過巴爾·發白諾克特加特基維儒特四人、呈請國府派充、（丙）通過購料委員會組織大綱、（四）臨時提案、（一）决定下星一上午十時、開第二次大會、（二）議决、所有英庚欵全數、以存入國家中央銀行爲原則、其詳細辦法另定之、（八日專電）

中央政治會議 3

修正黨員犯罪加重處罰法

通過監察院等本年度預算

（南京）　中央政治會議、八日晨八時、開第二六九次會議、于右任主席、茲探得議决各案如下、（一）請中央執行委員會將前經常務會議决議、暫緩公布之黨員犯罪加重處罰暫行法六條、重行提出討論、並請修正第四條爲「現任公務員、均以黨員論、但因公務員之身分、已特别規定加重處刑者、不得再行加重、」（二）通過監察院中央地政機關籌備處財政部緝私處直屬部隊等十九年度預算多起、（三）各省營業稅徵收條例、交經濟財政兩組審查、（八日中央社電）

（南京）　中政會經濟財政兩組、定十四日審查各省營業稅條例（八日中央社電）

川戰已告停頓 5

二劉改約在江津會晤

（南京）　川事鄧田兩部、麕集不過六萬人、鄧部較少、劉文輝部號稱八萬、劉湘號稱十二萬人、劉文輝經劉湘勸誘、可望不與鄧田一致、現在戰事停頓、俟江津會議結果如何再定、今日川電如下、（一）成都八日電、鄧錫侯田頌堯原來進攻李其相、係先得劉文輝同意、嗣劉湘迭電劉文輝、動以利害、說以叔姪之情、勸其趨向中

Page 4

央、維持和平、劉意稍動、乃存觀望、鄧田知勢孤、遂即停進、並請渝軍亦停進等語、（二）成都八日電、劉文輝電約劉湘、在　州會晤、劉湘復電云、只須有利於黨國、本人到省亦可、初不必一定在瀘、劉文輝改約江津晤面、十五前可成行、（三）成都八日電、楊森於川戰激烈時、擬率所部、向　中推進、現因雙方停戰狀態、改向達縣開進、（四）重慶七日電、此次戰事結果、劉湘部推展至武勝·大足·銅梁·璧山·合川五屬、劉文輝收編陳鴻文·陳鼎勉兩部、並佔有華陽簡陽兩屬、（八日）

（重慶）　渝劉湘令前敵各軍停止進攻後、田頌堯亦由省電駐順部隊、暫停前進、二劉决改地江津會商維持川局和平方法、川戰或可和平解决、（七日中央社電）

遼甯外交恊會 16

通過重要議案五項

（瀋陽）　遼國民外交協會五日至八日在瀋青年會開聯席會議、五日晨舉行開會式、每日討論會二次、外交常識講演一次、大會主席閻玉衡發表三日間議决案五條、（甲）贖回中東路案、（一）通電莫全權·於會議席上、誓死力爭、務必達到贖回中東路之目的、否則即請歸國、勿辱民命、（二）通電全國、主張立刻贖回中東路、（三）電各國聲明贖回中東路理由、（四）對蘇聯政府及民衆宣言、請其根據一九一九年及一九二零年宣言、並顧全國際信義、交還中東路、（五）組織贖回中東路委員會、内設調查基金評價三部、（乙）移民實邊案議决辦法、（一）奬勵内地同胞移居東北、（二）東北實况爲内地同胞所未悉、應請政府及各省法團聯合組織宣傳機關、以爲移民先導、（三）難民之來東北者地方政府及法團、應切實招待、並設法安置、使之各安其業、（四）要求中國紅十字會及紅卍字會對於東北移民接濟上特别注意、並撥大宗欵項以備應用、（五）要求各交通機關與難民以特别優待、（六）各省敎育當局應爲移民設特種學科、以立愛護東北之根基、（七）提倡農業合作宣傳運動、（八）肅清土匪以保護墾民、（九）由東北民衆聯合組織東北移民團體以便内地同胞、（丙）撤廢領事裁判權案議决辦法、（一）電請國府採取斷然手段無條件立刻的收回領事裁判權、（二）擴大撤廢領事裁判權宣傳運動督促政府迅速採取斷然手段、（丁）對俄通商復交應先有充分準備案、議决辦法、（一）通電全國國民注意、（一）俄人之反宣傳、（二）多方妨害内國工業發展、（三）陰謀破壞社會秩序擾亂治安、（二）請中央黨部實業部東北政務委員會各省黨部及實業團體組織大規模實業聯合經營辦法、（三）外交協會宜由小學中學方面入手、供給相當敎育材料、（一）中俄交涉歷史、使知俄人陰謀、不可爲其甘言所歆、（二）歷述粤湘贛赤禍之事實、使知共禍如洪水猛獸、（三）竭力宣傳三民主義以充實兒童之心、免赤色帝國主義之侵入、（戊）南滿鐵路問題案議决辦法、（一）提倡東北商工業、（二）自建東北鐵道網、（三）由大會委託東北出席國民會議代表提議交涉收回南滿鐵路及附屬地案、（八日中央社電）

時評

英邀德要人赴倫敦 22

英政府邀德總理及外長赴英集議。歐洲各國。今甚重視之。原夫英之所邀。不僅德之一國。在法雖未允赴。亦未拒絕。在意有謂亦在邀請之列。但以各國情勢之不同。故對於邀請。見解各異。在德國之意。正在德奥稅約議論紛紜之時。英旣未嘗表示劇烈之反對。而又有此邀請集會之舉。於外交上自屬有利而無害。故國内無分黨派。一致熱烈歡迎。柏林日報。且認爲歐戰後英德重行携手之表示。其贊成此舉。可想而知焉。

自歐戰以後。國際之聯合。幾有一定之方式不過戰勝之若干强國。互相分配。其餘之國。俯首受命而已。無所謂外交。更無所謂縱横捭闔之策也。自去年以來。德於國聯會中。稍稍露其頭角。博得各國之聲譽。迨至近來。乃有德奥稅約之發展。使國際呆滯之局勢。别開一生面。今又有英德非正式集會之舉動。歐洲外交之形勢。或將因是而有變動。宜乎各國之鄭重視之也。

兩國携手先聲

日期尙待商榷

法意被邀同時參加

白里安未明示拒絕

路透社七日巴黎電　英外相漢德森與德總理白魯寗外長寇蒂斯擬集議於倫敦一事、現仍爲一般人討論之事項、據可恃消息、英外相數星期前即以此事商諸法外長白里安、白並未謝絕之、但迄未答覆、蓋欲視國内政策之需要而裁覆也、衆料此次會議、將請他國、尤其是意國派員參加、

國民八日柏林電　德總理與外長赴英日期、英德政府間尚未商妥、前擬之五月一日及八日俱有障礙、英政府遂擬延至五月底、但德方不贊成、欲在國聯行政會開會以前相晤、故日期一層雙方仍在商榷中、

國民七日巴黎電　英政府之邀請法意德諸國政治家在倫敦作非正式之集會、實遠在二月中、此事茲已由法國某半官通信機關自法外部證實、但白里安當時並未立刻拒絕、即現在亦尙未答復、僅表示彼之能否與英德政治家相晤於吉可爾司英首相之别墅、須視海約起草之進展爲定云、在意國方面首相墨索里尼恐未必能赴英、但外長格蘭第或將代墨一行、亦有謂法外長之不願赴英、其主要原因之一、乃由英國在歐洲外交事務上久執牛耳、今若移樽就敎、將益增英國之聲勢、則白氏之地位、在法人眼光中恐不免受有影響、

國民七日柏林電　德國報紙不分黨派、對於總理白魯寗及外長寇蒂斯之接受英國邀請一節、皆表示極端欣忭、英國之邀請雖在德奥稅約事件發表之前、而此種私人聚談、在現時實較以前尤爲重要、因德奥稅約問題、勢必占談話之重要部分、而軍縮問題賠欵問題及俄國問題等等、恐反在其次也、柏林日報倫英政府之邀請、爲英人願與德人重行携手之表示、而德國世界報則謂白魯寗向來對於外交事務不願參與、而此次居然首肯赴英、則必胸有成竹、欲以友好之精神應付各問題、以挽德國之危局、而圖公共之利益、至於英人對德奥稅約之種種疑慮、亦不難以此行而袪除、英政治家發起斯舉、其誠意至堪欽佩云云、

山西整理金融會成立 81

太原通信、晋省整理金融設計委員會、昨日（三日）上午九時、在省府會議廳開成立會、出席者、計有省府主席商震、省府委員仇曾詒·常炳彝·馮司直·李尙仁·郭寳清、省黨部代表劉懷琪、第六軍軍長楊愛源、第五軍參謀長楊鳳麟、結果辦事處軍需組長郭殿屏、財政整理處代表楊培翹、商會代表王肇泰、錢業同業公會代表郝清照·段國楨、敎育會代表楊仁康、省銀行代表閻毓芹·李步青·常運文、及特聘委員高洪等十九人、商震主席、如儀行禮後、主席報告、略謂近來省鈔價格暴落、謠言紛起、物價增高、人民生活愈困、勞動界尤爲恐慌、軍費尙無着落、編遣費尙未撥來、恐因人心浮動、滋生事變、故金融之整理、實爲目下急切不容稍緩之要圖、整理金融之任務、省政府固責無旁貸、但以關係鉅大、情勢迫急、非集羣策羣力、不能善其後、故本席在省府會議提議、設立整理金融設計委員會、經議决由省黨部省政府各軍長結束辦事處軍需組財政整理處商會錢業同業公會敎育會農會省銀行及熟悉財政人員組織之、并通過辦法十條、定於今日成立、茲後每星期四上午開會一次、遇金融上發生特殊事故時、得開臨時會議、此即本會組織之起因、再者省府對於金融之整理、亦早已注意、第一次會議時、即將整理金融案提出討論、經議决電請中央、准予恢復金融公債、現在中央已交行政院核議、省委會第二次臨時會、又議决電催中央、速行核准、并電請張副司令速撥編遣費、并代催中央速核准金融公債辦法、茲奉張副司令東電、謂編費已令即日撥匯、催中央准予恢復金融公債電、亦已代發、但金融公債中央是否准予恢復、不能預斷、吾人必須自謀救濟之法、絕不能坐視金融之破産、使社會陷於擾亂、晋人遭罹浩刦、由此點觀之、本會更有設立之必要、總之本會組織之意義、即在於集羣策羣力、共謀本省金融問題之根本解决、以消弭未來之災禍、希望各機關各團體代表盡量發表卓見、以備省府採行云云、次由各機關各團體代表相繼發表意見、至十二時始散會、附錄該會組織辦法如下、（第一條）本委員會以研究救濟省鈔根本辦法、鞏固本省金融基礎爲範圍、定名爲整理金融設計委員會、（第二條）本委員會由省黨部·省政府·各軍長·結束辦事處軍需組·財政整理處·商會·錢業同業公會·敎育會·農會·省銀行·及由省政府推定之熟習本省財政人員組織之、（第三條）前列各機關、至少須派一人出席、各軍長得派代表出席、（第四條）本委員會設於省政府内、（第五條）本委員會以每星期四上午九時至十一時爲會議時間、但遇金融上發生特殊事故時、得由省政府召集臨時會議、（第六條）各機關及各委員、均得隨時提出建議書、其建議書之審查整理、由大會隨時推定負責人員辦理之（第七條）本委員會議决事項、得隨時建議於省政府、（第八條）本委員會承辦事務·及繕寫紀錄人員、得就各機關臨時調用之、（第九條）本委員會委員概不支薪、至會内必需之辦公費、得由省政府隨時撥付、（第十條）本辦法自省政府委員會議决之日施行、

吳鐵城在哈之談話 82

視察三日然後赴黑

哈爾濱通訊、視察東北黨務之吳鐵城、四月一日早八時、自吉林蒞哈、擬在哈居住三日、七日下午赴黑龍江、在黑亦擬住三日、然後回遼、轉道平津、預定四月下旬歸京、吳抵哈時、各界領袖及機關要人、均到車站歡迎、狀况極爲熱烈、吳現住秦家崗大直街護路軍總司令行轅、各要人往訪甚衆、是日吳與新聞記者談話如下、（問）東北黨務公開後、外交上有無問題、（答）無問題、中國人辦中國的黨、外人無干涉權、不過黨務辦起、外人不願意并的確十分恐懼、（問）哈市成立黨部後、東鐵華員是否須入黨、因東鐵具有外交關係、華員入黨與否、蘇俄甚爲注意、（答）此則聽其自然、絕不勉强、但希望其入黨、（問）東鐵華員如入黨後、尙另組黨部否、（答）亦歸地方黨部辦理、不另設黨部、（問）先生對東北黨務有何意見、（答）希望各黨部依照文化宣傳兩點、努力作去、此外則本造林造路衛生保甲提倡國貨七項工作進行、因文化可提高人民程度、宣傳可使人民認識本黨、其他爲一般工作、則各黨部自須實施、（問）中央是否派員帮同東北辦黨、（答）中央對東北黨務、悉聽憑地方辦理、不加干涉、但願依照中央方針進行、（問）此地黨委祇有三人在哈、黨部即成立否、（答）待大家商量决定、惟願在本人未離哈前、得觀厥成、（問）對民衆入黨、有何辦法、（答）未入黨者、以一年爲期、目爲準備黨員、（問）官吏如何、（答）文官科長、武員少校以上、或須入黨、但亦未一定云云、

吳氏現經各團體之約、定五日午後四時、在道外禮拜堂公開講演黨務問題、至哈市黨部、頃附設特區長官公署内、正式成立時、則覔一相當地點、又黨委鄒尙友、已隨津市長張學銘赴津、聞遺席尙須由中央另派、（四日）

工廠法推行問題 103

工商管理協會定十一

日開會討論

在展緩施行之工廠、法修改問題、各方提案、共計七案之多、經工商管理協會幾度討論、曾以工商管理協會一案、爲最精確、惟經分發各廠商研究後、多數意見、尙擬修正、茲悉本星期六、工商管理會、擬再彙集討論、以爲最後之决定、記者復以工廠法推行租界外國工廠問題、及與國聯勞工局之關係、訪中華工業總聯會錢承緒君、詢以經過歷史、答稱、一九一九年、中國簽訂德奥和約、即爲國防勞動組織之會員、一九一九年勞工大會在華盛頓開會、特别國委員會、曾討論遠東各國勞工問題、其關於中國部分、希望、（一）中國政府採取以工廠法保護工人之原則、（二）主張國際勞工大會、向有關係各國交涉、使其在華享有之租界及租界地内、仿照中國政府已定之勞工法、將由中國政府在租界及租借地内執行、一九二三年三月、中國政府根據該會之主張、頒布工廠暫行條例、其第三條明白規定、凡在中國領域内、外國工廠、均應一律適用、而其租界當局、即起恐慌、疊次集議、對於此節主張、（一）租界僅採用工廠條例原則之一部分、另訂租界工廠單行條例、（二）治外法權未經撤廢以前、暫緩考慮、（三）中國政府如允接受童工委員會之意見、修政條例、并能在江浙兩省或僅江蘇一省内實行、租界工部局將設法取得必要之權、任令施行於租界、嗣以各方意見紛岐、無形中止、一九一八年國勞局長多瑪來華觀光、中國政府重申前議、其時工商部已訂工廠法草案、多瑪以未得授權答之、一九二九年、國勞開十二次大會、中國政府代表、再度提出「外人在華工廠應服從中國政府施行之勞工法案」之建議、以票數不足、致遭否决、議者復叩以本届勞工大會、貴會旣改派代表、對於本案、代表團要否提出、答稱、事權在於政府、非僱主代表能單獨行動云、

在還本前十天抽籤 113

修正後之市公債逾本辦法

上海市政府、前准上海市市政公債基金保管委員會公函、以國民政府所發之各種公債、均將抽籤日期、定於各該條例、而修正市公債條例、僅於第八條規定還本日期、而抽籤日期、則未規定、若每次臨時酌定、似不足以昭劃一、擬請在每年三月三十一日、及九月三十日、以前一個月内、預定一抽籤日期、至應否將預定抽籤日期、追加於條例之内、并祈裁奪等因、市政府業已函復該會、謂市公債條例、業經本府呈准修正、可不必再將抽籤日期添入條例之内、嗣後舉行抽籤、應根據向例、於還本期前十日舉行可也云云、上海市政公債之還本辦法、原定前十二期每期還本二十萬元、後二期每期還本三十萬元、市政府因此項數目、與抽籤數目不相符合、呈請行政院、轉咨立法院修正、業經政府公布在案、查修正條例之還本辦法、爲前十二期每期抽七籤、每籤還三三萬元、共計各還二十一萬元、最後二期、每期抽八籤、每籤還本三萬元、共計各還二十四萬元、至其利息、則原爲一百十八萬八千元、照修正條例、僅須利息一百十五萬四千四百元、計减少利息三萬三千六百元、於持票人旣有利益、而市民負擔、亦可因以减輕云、

已故葉澄袁之孫葉仲芳、混名小抖亂、前年與曾充甘維露律師繙譯後赴無錫被匪殺害之陳志剛之女陳秀珍非正式結合、嗣被髮妻陸氏得悉、詬誶頻加、葉始感覺妻妾之間難爲夫之痛苦、遂棄甜蜜之家庭、遠適異鄉、度枯寂之生活、而置家事於不顧矣、邇則葉妻陸氏、因所天之出亡、純由秀珍所造就、特控之於法公廨、而秀珍之母陳嚴氏、因葉家住膠州路、亦延薛嘉圻律師向特區地方法院控告葉仲芳誘姦其女、原狀如下、

訴狀原文　爲被告連續意圖姦淫和誘未滿二十歲女子脫離享有親權之人觸犯刑法第二五七條第二項之罪、提起自訴事、謹將被告犯罪事實陳述於左、緣自訴人之親生女陳秀珍、現年十九歲、前在上海嫦娥跳舞塲爲舞女、易名雪莉、當民國十八五月間、被告時至該舞塲跳舞、因與秀珍相識、𧰟秀珍貎麗、即蓄意和誘、時偕赴其在梵王宫旅社及滄洲飯店内之房問游玩、親近口久、被告遂施誘衛、以富有家財眩惑秀珍、並謂與妻不睦、當與離婚後迎娶爲正妻、種種詐騙、於民國十八年　歷六七月間和誘秀珍至遠東飯店闢室姦宿、以後時開旅館房間續姦、秀珍其時年僅十七、意志薄弱、受其誘惑後、仍隠瞞不告自訴人、直至同年十二月廿二晨、被告忽來自訴人家中訪晤秀珍後、詭託同出進早餐即回、不料一去不返、杳如黄鶴、候至廿五日、自訴人曾投法租界盧家灣巡捕房報告拐逃、詎知被告誘走秀珍、偕宿於新新社十一號房間、至同月廿六日、租屋於福煦路明德里四十五號二層樓、迄去歲一日十七日、被告偕秀珍同至蔣保釐律師處、簽訂夫妾契約、（共三紙、各執一紙、其餘一紙在蔣律師處、）後秀珍始回家、告知經過情形、自訴人詰悉秀珍早失身於被告、木已成舟、無法挽回、祗得容忍、孰料本年三月一日、被告忽因與秀珍吵鬧失和、送回自訴人家中、遺棄不顧、嗾使其母葉彭氏·其妻陸嬰蘭·虚搆被告失戀出亡事實、延請律師誣訴秀珍詐財傷害、藉報紙宣傳、爲恐嚇自訴人之方法、此爲被告犯罪之事實、伏按秀珍現年十九歲、尙未成年、依法應受自訴人之監護、被告竟迭背訴人誘其出外　宿、顯然觸犯刑法第二五七條二項意圖姦淫而和誘未滿二十歲女子脫離親權享有之人之罪、自訴人雖於事後覺察容忍、然亦不足爲其違法性之阻却、爲此具狀提起自訴仰祈鈞院迅賜票拘被告葉仲芳到案審判、按法科刑、至爲德便、謹狀、

請求展期　法院據狀、原定本月六日午後閉審、嗣因是日適値節期乃復改爲昨日午後二時、由蕭爕蔡推事開第三法庭傳訊、原告陳嚴氏翠女秀珍偕代理律師薛嘉圻·等如期到庭、被告葉仲芳不到、延江一平·董俞·兩律師辯護、據　律師謂被告於本案發生之前、已經離滬、其家屬接奉傳票、即委託江律師登報通告審期、但今仍未回申、應　展期、以便再行通告云云、

改期續訊　蕭推事旋傳陳嚴氏訊問年籍住址據該氏稱、現年四十歲住法租界　母院路廣順里十九號、其律師遂墏最近被告致陳女一函提出、詎明被告已知被控顯係故意避不投案、應請拘究蕭推事以被告不應畏避不到、姑念初次開庭諭再改期本月廿三午後續訊、届時倘猶避匿當予拘提、陳嚴氏等遂皆退去、　　十六封信　聞葉自聞被控猶仍與陳秀珍頻通尺素、積至目今、秀珍已獲其親筆信函、有十六封之多、雖俱不書明發信地點、然審視郵避於信封上所蓋之戳則知其都係寄自南京或浦口兩地、僅一封係在北平付郵、而各信措詞什九含懺悔悲哀之意、可見其滿腹牢騷、無從宣洩、不覺流露於字裏行間、就中復有數函、則附有另件、如在北平所發者其内附新聞報快活林最近所刊「一封情書抵得一篇𧰟情小說」之記事一段、又信附有報紙所登「落花有意流水無情」之廣告一張、並於其背後註「我和你的結果、如此可憐的過去、不堪回首、」數語、

兩張照片　附有照片者則有兩函、一附虎丘劍池照片一幀、另於片面書「去年今日此門中·人面桃花相映紅·人面不知何去處·桃花依舊笑東風·」崔護所作之詩一首、片後加註係吐血方痊、扶病攝就、送作紀念等語、此信寄自南京、其信封之「背面」書曰、去年同游·今年獨溜·重念前塵·棲慘·莉、我一生愛的人、我和你相戀了如許日、不幸竟分散了、這張照是吐血扶病拍的、所以不像我送你做個紀念罷一附長僅寸許闊約三分葉仲芳本入坐於黄包車上所拍之照、另附數語於信封背面云、信封内這照、是我投考前拍的、此後我也許生存、也許死亡、也許這是我最後的一張照了、剪下送給你、不知你願受否、心愛的人兒、又於照片背面上寫、莉、你若仍愛我、請你將這照保留、仲、

最近一信　四月四日又自京寄一信云、莉、在不幸中碰見了上海來的熟人、無法躱避中、站在街頭、談了好久、他說你在最近、又加請了逖百克處姚先生了、（唉、我一生的友人、爲什麽公事公辦的人兒、佔了多數呢、世情、）其實這又何必呢、我在南京時、已託人打過長途電話、要求家裏撤銷訴訟了、他又說、特區法院爲了你母親控我的緣故、要我到庭對質了、本來、我現在是着了製服的人了、是個只受軍事法裁判的人了、但我爲了要在明鏡的推事前、表白我現在心中的　苦和酸楚、在必要時、我决心的設法告假回上海來、我將以這瘦削像鬼一様的臉、和你相見於我不願見你的地方了、唉、悽慘、莉啊、你是打定主意、和我走散了、以前你是不要記憶了、以後、你是追隨着了「他姓」去了、唉、我痴愛着的人兒啊、你是一切不願的去了、只　下了我一個、呆子似的、望前想後、世間最慘痛的事、没有比這個再利害了、不久、也許我要見你了、在見你時、你能允許我和你談幾句嗎、這是我一生唯一的希望了、想到將在何處見你、心中又難過起來了、我正自慚、爲何没有勇氣自殺呢、死了、一切就完了、心裏難過得很、寫不下去了、回過以前、好像一塲春夢而已、唉、再會罷、祝你前途光明幸福無景、

被竊夏布人造絲

失竊貨額　此次阜生輪出口、有本埠悅來公報裝運赴烟台（Ｓ２生利嘜）之夏布六十六件、又有ＶＹＫ牌子之人造絲一件、統係自滬往芝罘交卸者、該貨因係貴重品、故當下船時、即令裝入保險艙内、以示愼重、該貨在七日夜中下船、至昨晨即發見被竊、逆料係在七日之下半夜被竊、

報警緝查　此次失竊之六十七件貨物、估計價値約在六千餘兩、當時船員等在船澈查無着、即報告總行、一方面通知東悅公報關行、以損失過巨、而且保險艙中貨失竊、殊妨碍以後之運輸、遂由怡和及東悅公報告水陸警察及租界捕房偵緝、並貨主出賞格購緝、如有知風通報因而破案者、賞洋百元、如能將該貨緝獲者、則照貨價百分之十賞給、

縣基路閣老坊、建於遜清良熙初年、係跨路建築、對於交通方面、頗多妨礙、且因年代過久、失於修理、殘缺零落、時虞傾圯、而其上層石料、自經一度火焚之後、大部份均已脆碎、即欲修理、亦已無從着手、本市市政當局、前因該處路西房屋、已經翻造改進、路東舊屋、亦待拆讓、該坊險象百出、任其孤立路中、設被重車碰揰、其上層石料、隨時均可倒坍、爲公共安全及便利交通着想、不如從早拆卸、現聞閣老坊業於前日全部拆竣、所有拆下石料、均交由坊裔徐承宗等保存、市政府並以該坊原係紐紀念明大學士徐光啓而建、爲留永久紀念起見、已將縣基路更名爲光啓路、以示於整理市政之中、仍不失追念先哲之意云、

華中隊 170

守門　全隊中之佼佼者、穏健可取於是前之嚴重壓迫下、能維持至此者、洵非易事、最後之失、非戰之罪也、

後衛　華中隊之最弱點、失脚無算、球去無方、

中衛　中堅虞克定甚佳、時有甚妙之接濟、惜兩前衛亦過弱、退不足守、進不能攻、

前鋒　出類拔萃當推袁慶武、王以德有遲滯之病、兩　雖勇、奔走不速、心有餘、力不足、綜觀兩隊、普通大病、即在舉動不速、更以華中爲甚、不往尋球、而專坐而等待、是爲不可能、而射球無方向、尤爲不能大大得意原因、失球爲最危險之事、能制全軍死命、兩隊後衛竟時見之、此數端似中以健兒應努力者也、雖然、一時集合、能有若是成績非易易矣、

第一次中等學校聯合運動會 177

—四月二十四日至二十六日三天—

長程賽跑會四月十九晨十時舉行

上海市敎育局令市立及私立立案試辦改良各中等學校云、本局爲促進本市各中等學校、及全市市民之體育起育起見、業經定期舉行上海市第一次中等學校聯合運動會、及長程賽跑會、並經分别擬定競賽規程、及賽跑會規則、呈奉市政府第九六九八號指令内開、「呈件均悉、應予照准、仰即由該局分别公布施行可也、此令、件存、等因、奉此、自應公佈施行、除分别函令外、合亟抄同規程規則各一份、令仰知照、此令、附抄發競賽規程及賽跑會規則各一份、

上海市第一次長程賽跑會規則

第一條　本會以促進全市市民體爲宗旨、

第二條　凡本市市民除以體育爲職業者外、年滿十六歲以上、均得來會參加比賽、

第三條　本會賽跑路徑爲環繞南市三路圓路電車路缐兩周計程一萬一千米、

第四條　本會於四月十九日上午十時舉行比賽

第五條　本會設會長一人總幹事總裁判員各一人、計數員評判員辦事員各若干人、辦理一切事務、

第六條　各運動員比賽時、應完全按照本會所定路線前進、如有跑錯路線、應仍回原錯處重跑、途中不得踏上行人道或请人扶持、或阻碍他運動員前進、

第七條　各運動員得自請引導員一人引進、但以乘自由車者爲限、「引導員言待運動員到小南門口時方可引導、」

第八條　比賽優勝員額定十五名、其在十五名以外、而能在一小時内跑完全程者、亦給予紀念物品、

第九條　比賽事宜由總裁判主持之、凡總裁判之判决各運動員、不得抗議、

第十條　本規則自市敎育局呈奉市政府核准公佈後施行、

上海市第一次中等學校聯合運動會競賽規程 178

第一條　本會由市敎育局主辦、以促進全市中等學校之體育爲宗旨、

第二條　凡市内公立及私立已立案之中等學校、皆得選派學生爲本會運動員、凡經市敎育局核准試辦或改良之私立中等學校、得呈准市敎育局選派學生爲本會運動員、

第三條　本會會塲借用勞神父路中華全國體育協進會田徑賽塲、

第四條　本會開會日期自二十年四月二十四日起至二十六日止、遇必要時、得由本會會長决定變更之、

第五條　本會設會長一人、副會長一人、會務主任一人、主持一切會務、

第六條　本會會務分事務競技二部、每部各設主任一人、事務部分庶務會計文牘編輯招待糾察六股、競技部分競賽塲地二股、各股職員名額、由會務主任視事務之繁簡酌定後、呈由會長委聘之、

第七條　運動員競賽分男女兩部、其項目如左、（甲）男子部、「田賽」跳高、跳遠、撑竿跳高、三級跳遠、擲鐵餅、擲標槍、推十二磅鉛球、「徑賽」百米、二百米、四百米、八百米、一千五百米、五千米、百十米高欄、四百米低欄、八百米替換賽跑、一千六百米替換賽跑、（乙）女子部、「田賽」跳高、跳遠、擲標槍、推八磅鉛球、「徑賽」五十米、百米二百米四百米替換賽跑、

第八條　每運動員報認運動、除替換賽跑外、男子以四項爲限、女子以三項爲限、每校每部每項以四人爲限、

第九條　比賽規章按照中華全國體育協進會比賽規則辦理、

第十條　本會錦標共分四種、計男女團體及男女個人各二種、

（一）團體錦標　以得分最多之學校得之、遇兩個以上之學校得分相等時、以得第一名較多者决定之、

（二）個人錦標　以得分最多之運動員得之、遇兩以上分數相等時、以得第一名較多者决定之、

自由談

世界小事記 179

— 海客

▲荷蘭京城亞姆斯透旦Amsterdam城中。有幾處多風的街角冬天很爲寒冷。因此市政當局將一種板裝在巡警站崗處的地下。通以電流。日夜温暖。使巡警站在那裏。不致有手脚氷凍之苦。

▲倫敦惠斯敏士Westminster鐘塔中的大鐘。BigBen是世界著名大鐘之一。在一千八百五十八年初掛起來的時候。就有了裂痕。不然。報時的聲浪可以達到二十英里以外。

▲英國銀行是英國的國家銀行。所有鈔票用紙。專在哈姆府Hampshire一家紙廠中製造。工人們除在他自已工作的所在可以出入時。不許闖入别的工場以免流弊。

▲美國新新南底Cincinnatl城中。有姊妹四人。都是孿生的。嫁人後所生的子女。也都是孿生。尤其有趣的。内中有兩位姊妹。各得兩對孿生的子女。

▲坎那大也是世界富饒之區。金鑛常有發見。曾有一處。計長一千英里。竟好像是一條極長的金帶。

漁會歸來 180

— 葉華女士

江洋湖海·浩淼莫測·介鱗滋生·利不可勝計也。吾國密犧氏結網罟。敎佃漁。漁業發明。遠在上古。奈蚩蚩漁氓囿於智識。拙於技術。漁法則父作子述多年無改。漁具則新信舊製。永不更張企業心薄弱。浮家泛宅。志在一飽。坐視生計日蹙。强鄰乘隙。以我爲弋。鼓輪如織魚業不修。累及海疆門户。念此阽危隐憂曷已茲者江蘇農礦廳。上海市社會局曁省市黨部委員有鑒及此。組設改進漁業會、爲擴大運動計、訂本月四日至十日、在滬假民立中學、開改進漁業宣傳會今記一二。以饗閱者。

▲中國漁塲面積及捕魚能力　該會統計報告。謂全球魚塲面積共一百六十七萬九千零五十二方浬。中國則爲二十七萬一千八百零五方浬。占世界第一位外人估計吾國海洋可産四萬萬六千二百零六萬元然今捕魚能力不及十分之一。現吾國漁獲額僅二萬萬零八百元。其中華人自捕者猶不得四分之一。餘皆日人所有。能不痛心。

▲大連灣中日漁民獲物比較　招待某向　來賓聲稱。大連日漁民祇百餘。華人十倍之。而所得尙不及日人十分之一、覘上年十一月分中日漁民獲物比較。中國撈獲數量爲三十萬四百四十斤。金額二萬二千七百零六元。日本數量爲二百七十五萬四千六百九十四斤金額十三萬九千四百十九元旅居大連日人常傲然曰。中國漁塲需彼開發願國人思之重思之。　　▲各海魚類及外洋水産輸入　年來歐美漁港。鱗次櫛比。吾國東海多黄魚綢魚東海黄海間與渤海灣産小黄魚。黄海則𫓾魚、　魚、帶魚南海則大帶魚。　魚依照總理計劃各海岸應闢魚塲魚港。良以此無盡藏之寳庫。足以阜民生而裕國計第計劃未現罟網天利操諸外人。十八年水産進口總數。達二百六十八萬八千六百五十九擔。總金額凈數關平銀二千七百五十二萬五千八百二十八兩。此項經濟上之損失。亦不可謂不鉅矣。

▲綠儁赤儁二頭龜身大如船　展覽室共十。陳列多海洋氣象航海物漁具釣具。各國新式漁船圖及網具曁水産製造品等。綜觀各室以吾國漁塲模型。虽天鏡。天文鐘及貝扣堆成之國徽、尤爲罕見。綠𧓈龜及赤𧓈龜。身大如船。允稱奇物。又黄魚一尾。重約四十餘斤。身長丈餘。碩大無朋。據云十年間僅得一二尾。其膏肚。價百金。推滋補上品。

▲不費分文人人有得魚機會　此次分送入塲劵二萬。三千劵有贈品。來賓參觀畢。持劵向贈品處摸彩。　魚。烏賊。小黄魚。明蝦等色色俱備。全恃命運。余與張仰高王德昌見某校三十餘人僅獲小黄魚二尾。餘悉空票。而民立中學註册主任張鑫長五劵中。摸得　魚鯊魚各一。見者健羨不止。

桃花之種種 181

— 楊一笑

▲桃花鹽　生於琴湖池此鹽色如桃花。隨月之大小而盈縮。

▲桃花醋　有一種桃花醋。唐世風俗所貴重。若醋溜黄魚。糖醋鯽魚等。略用少許。其味比鎭江醋更鮮美。

▲桃花米　松江桃花山。産桃花米。粒粒皆作桃紅之色。入鑊内煑熟爲飯、趁熱食之。軟糯香艶。别有風味。

▲桃花粉　婦人香粉内。以胭脂調匀。名桃花粉。倒之掌中。薄敷兩頰。艶若飛霞矣。

别開生面之紙鳶官司 182

— 黄影呆

當此春光駘蕩之天。滬上房屋林立。每苦無放紙鳶之地。不若鄉村則田之間草野之中、隨處皆宜。於是滬地兒童。見有拆屋翻造處即視爲放紙鳶佳地、課餘之閒。咸持各色紙鳶。迎風向空而放。五光十色映射於金黄色日光之中别有奇觀。惟偶一不愼、紙鳶翻身、而電桿木上之電缐、情面毫無、必使紙鳶粉身碎骨而後已。此乃滬人放鳶之不便。我校附近有曠塲一。亦爲拆屋翻造處。日暖風和之天。塲中日必有無數兒童。爭放紙鳶。因使我憶及去年香港發生之一塲紙鳶官司。個中情形。彌可發噱。蓋香港境内、華人不少。每至春日。兒童之放紙鳶者、亦大不乏人。惟香港一地。自强英割去後。一切市政專權。悉操於英人之手。對於兒童嬉戲。有時亦受當局干涉去年香港有一兒童放紙鳶時。爲當局所拘。開庭辬論。亦有律師出庭。以律師而辦理放紙鳶件。殆亦别開生面之事也。法庭方面。以此童在魯濱遜街放紙鳶時。曾損環電報綫及某姓坡璃窗。實爲違法。蓋嬉戲之事。有碍居民或行人者。法律載明當局亦有禁止之權。然被告律師。要求證明放紙鳶一事。是否列入嬉戲。並詢廷上此次所傷者何人。所損者何物。法官謂並未傷人惟無論如何。放紙鳶而觸及電綫。必爲違法之事律師又詢其此種法律。係根據何條、並請當庭檢出、詎法官將律書遍翻一過。竟無此種法律。因而一塲紙鳶官司。終於宣告無罪。

人工造金魚法 183

— 吳吉人

不佞愛金魚成癖。前年供職杜美路明星總公司時文牘部同仁。嘗晋我以金魚博士之徽號。過承藻飾。更不敢負愛我者之一番美意。於是博訪周諮。採集關於藝魚之材料。藉供一般同嗜者之採納焉。

一咋子夜。與王獻齋君訪東三省影片經理郭于兩君於中央四樓。于君魯人。即詢以藝魚之術。蓋我國金魚。生長魯省。以濟寗濟南兩縣出産爲大宗。此則不佞所親歷而目覩者也于君飽學之士。語誠不虚。于君之言曰、君等僅知金魚爲卵生實不知人工亦可種植也。余甚訝之。于謂金魚之原始實與蠅蛃之類相伯仲。旣可卵生復可濕生、卵生則孵卵耳。人工則甚覺奇特。法以　蠶子入水。水無庸大。經需經丈之池即可。池底有泥。下蠶子其間。任其受日光曝之。使陰雨連朝。亦聽之可也。一俟大伏過後。水底游魚。千百成羣。日飼以水蛆。便長大矣。于君又謂欲金魚成紅色。則取黄蠶種下之。欲其成白。則下白種。欲其紅白相間。則取花蠶種亦如之。余初不之信。繼而于引證禮記月令是月也腐草化爲螢一語。余始恍然。尙有藝魚術。未便多佔自由篇幅。已付刊「新家庭」月刊矣。

節物偶談（二） 184

— 天虚我生

紙鳶之設。乃使小兒仰面夫内熱。亦以袪病爲目的。一年之中。在氣候變換時。人身氣血亦即起大變調故老年人往往在二至二分。及四立時節。大發舊病。小兒體質薄弱。正與老人衰弱者同故於令節。必有一二預防時疾之藥餌。用於食物中。但皆　焉而不察耳。清明之麥苗。即其一例用以袪除内熱。其效用正與紙鳶同。宫室之中。承塵往往藻繪極工。亦正使萬畿叢睉之身。常得仰面嘘氣。以袪五中煩熱。元夜張燈。其時在立春後。亦使萬人昂首而觀。袪其内熱。用意至爲微妙。然而吾人終歲埋頭。則未免太不衛生矣。

清明插柳。俗謂切魂以予推想。殊不謂然。西槳以柳醲治熱病。及解血毒極效。柳酸即自柳條之嫩皮中提出。亦稱沙利先酸。清明節後。則楊柳生花。柔條變老。所含養分。尸都消失。故在清明前折取之。插於門外。所以使以使行人旅客之取用也。其用意。亦爲治療天花水痘而設。凡患痘症。忽而回落。不能透發。則熱毒内陷。其人必死。若以水楊柳煎湯　拭。則痘粒立即復顯。紅潤飽滿。熱毒由毛孔排洩而出。無不活者。如在天花流行時。以此煎服。則清熱解毒。能利小便。引熱下行尤治痢疾。但以清明插褚柳葉煎服良效故予以爲此等設備。正與端午插蒲艾於門。所以便行人之中暑患痧者同。又小兒以清明柳條作圈。套於頸項。蓋以防喉痧瘰𤻤癤瘍諸症。頭爲衆陽之首。頸則百脉所經。亦取柳酸能解血毒。使自毛孔入也。以柳圈套之狗頸。則狗好弄。必去其圈嚙之。亦以防止　狗與瘋狗而已。

印度遊記（十八） 185

— 靈花

印度之運動。近英國已大受打撃。所有英貨一律不用。他國亦受影響。惟東洋方面。日本貨爲之暢銷。以海關論。從前日可收一百三五十萬稅。今則减至三五十萬。一日减去一百萬。其受打撃可知。現大都會尙可收房捐。鄉下抗稅甚盛。不易收也。有印人一開木匠店者告我。其廠内昔百五十工人。今止十人。商業之衰可知。英人所僱印人當兵者多屬於尼泊爾人。十之七八。至總數難確知。或云四五十萬尼泊爾人强悍。英人僱以當兵。故英人不能以兵力制尼泊爾也。尼泊爾八曾助英於歐戰。以勇顯於歐洲。未可輕視。今英人入藏阻其路者。惟尼泊爾也。至不丹小邦。亦佛敎國。然久爲英保護。道階法師言。不丹國佛像甚美今北境惟此兩佛敎國。南境惟一錫蘭島耳。

印度將來有問題其在士爾基乎。印度西北境盡回敎諸國。現在未能全助印人者。以阿富汗等國。尙爲王國與英尙有同情。然其人民頗與印民聯絡接濟。有一大問題即土爾基之鐵道將延長而通至波斯地方。此鐵道爲從君士坦丁來者其欵爲土德俄三國之欵北路通。則俄德土之勢力可聯合也。波斯境近印度西部之孟買地方土爾基自改爲共和政體後。國勢亦强。未可侮也。

五號。在大學校長室開東方文化恊會。TheLeagueorOrientalCulture由校長Ruthkrishna主席。及中國學敎授巴立齋博士等提議。其外各大學敎授二十人。發起人中有波斯人。甚　研東方文化。欲約予赴太戈爾大學。此會初名亞洲文化同盟會余因余有東方文藝復興會之紐組織主張合并。亞洲不如東方二字之含渾衆贊成余議改用東方。將來可出報。并派人到中國聯絡交換智識。但余提問東方文化之意義究竟如何。應稍有目標。方有價値。余言谂今爲物質主義世界。主張唯物者爲馬克司派。若主張新學。已不成問題。必歸淘汰也。如余所主張。係主張生命主義。唯生論者所以不論如何。尙可與馬克司唯物派鼎峙。因唯物不能算完全終以生命要緊。我以爲東方文化之目標。不如建在生命生活上。爲理由優長。印僧史那　君亦贊成余論。方免玄學鬼之譏。至如何聯络之處。以各國問互換智識爲第一步云。

晨間釐市仍緊 189

市塲概况　目前洋厘勢漸呈緊象、人心愈趨愈俏、更兼客銷胃口、日常踴躍勿稍替、市上頭襯縱不覺枯窘、要亦不無支肘之慮、銀行方面爲維持鈔票準備計亟應有所未雨綢繆、故雖現欵充裕、然一經各方之羅掘、宜其不大漲而亦循序升騰焉、

厘拆價格　（洋厘）早市厘價突又超出新高價、爲七錢二分六厘三毫七忽半、較前日又好三毫七忽半、午市仍恢復其原有市價、爲七錢二分六厘、觀其趨勢、依然有升高可能、（銀拆）早市三分、午市二分、較前日又復遞降一分、劃頭仍無加水而爲白劃、銀行頭襯充斥不堪、無人問津　　輔幣市情　江南小洋、供求雙方均屬有限、故市價勿動、仍與前日同價、爲六錢四分、而交易略較前日稍多、計早市六千角、午市四千五百角廣東小洋早市爲六錢四分二厘、午市爲六錢四分一厘半　、做出交易、早市十五萬角、午市七萬五千角、銅元則加長一千文爲三百七十千○五百文、交易有限、僅二萬七千餘串、

青年園地稿例 206

（一）文字以關於青年問題之討論、國内國外學校成學生之消息·隨筆·學校生活之描寫·筆　等爲範圍、體裁不拘

（二）圖　以關於青年問題者爲限、

（三）照片以青年生活、（如運動·旅行·进覽·演劇演講·集會·展覽各種比賽等）學校新聞及青年運動等爲合格、不論個人團體、均所歡迎　　（四）稿紙勿寫兩面、

（五）文字每篇字數至多不得過二千、

（六）稿勿横寫、字勿潦草、西文可省則省如不得已須引用原文、須附於譯文之下、

（七）圖　勿用藍墨水繪、並勿用有色之紙、須用白紙黑繪、

（八）來稿請書明青年園地編輯部收、

（九）來稿無論刊載與否、概不退還、如須退還、應預先聲明、

（十）酬資文字每千字分三元·二元·一元三種、圖　照片每幅亦同此例、如有特别之稿、酬資另計、

Domestic Important Telegrams

British Boxer Indemnity Board of Trustees 2

Announced its Establishment Yesterday

Hoare Elected Vice Chairman

Drawing Lots to Determine the Term of Office of Trustees

(Nanjing) The Board of Trustees for the Administration of the British Returned Boxer Indemnity was formally announced established on the morning of the 8th. The first general meeting was held at 10:00 AM in the conference hall of the Ministry of Railways. The Chinese side was represented by Zhu Jia-hua, Chen Qi-cai, Li Shu-hua, Cheng Zhen-jun, Ye Gong-chuo, Wang Jia-zhen, Huang Han-liang, Song Zi-liang, and Zeng Rong-fu. The British side was represented by Hore-Belisha, Durnford, and ten others, twelve in total. First, Chairman Zhu reported that the council was established by order of the National Government to handle the British returned Boxer Indemnity, and reported the amount and use of accumulated and unmatured funds. Because there were many proposals, the meeting had not concluded by 1:30 PM, so it was temporarily suspended. Chairman Zhu invited the trustees to lunch at the League of Nations Society. The meeting continued at 4:00 PM and adjourned at 6:30 PM. Immediately afterwards, the first meeting of the Standing Committee of Directors was held, and the Vice Chairman, Secretary, Accountant, and Wang Jia-zhen were elected to draft meeting rules and detailed procedures. The proceedings were as follows: (1) The term of office of the directors was determined by drawing lots as follows: one year: Wang Jia-zhen, Song Zi-liang, Hore, Massie, Chen Qi-cai; two years: Li Shu-hua, Kentley, Ye Gong-chuo, Cheng Zhen-jun, Zeng Rong-fu; three years: Durnford, Zeng Yang-fu, Brone, Huang Han-liang, Zhu Jia-hua. (2) Hore was elected Vice Chairman, Huang Han-liang was elected Secretary, and Zeng Rong-fu was elected Accountant. (3) Matters for discussion: (A) To pass a resolution that the Board should establish a Standing Committee of Directors; (1) To determine the number of members of the Standing Committee to be seven; (2) It was decided that the Chairman, Vice Chairman, Secretary and Accountant should be the ex-officio members of the Standing Committee, and Ye Gong-chuo, Wang Jia-zhen and Brone were elected as members of the Standing Committee. (B) The selection of members of the Purchasing Committee: according to the provisions of the agreed exchange of documents, there should be six members, in addition to the Chinese diplomatic representative in the UK and the representative of the Ministry of Railways, the remaining four members should be recommended by the British government, and then the Chinese government should select four members to be members, and it was agreed that Barr, Fairburn, Blockade, and Jewett should be appointed to the National Government. (C) To pass the outline of the Purchasing Committee organization. (4) Temporary proposals: (1) To decide to hold the second general meeting at 10:00 AM next Monday. (2) Resolved that, in principle, all British Boxer Indemnity funds should be deposited in the National Central Bank, and detailed measures will be determined separately. (8th day Special Dispatch)

Central Political Conference 3

Amends Law on Increased Punishment for Party Members' Crimes

Passes This Year's Budget for the Control Yuan and Others

(Nanjing) The Central Political Conference held its 269th meeting at 8:00 AM on the 8th, chaired by Yu Youren. The resolutions are as follows: (1) To request the Central Executive Committee to re-submit for discussion the six articles of the Interim Law on Increased Punishment for Party Members' Crimes, which were temporarily suspended from promulgation by the previous Standing Committee meeting, and to amend Article 4 to "Incumbent civil servants shall be deemed party members, but if there are special provisions for increased punishment due to their status as civil servants, no further increase shall be made." (2) To pass the budget for the Control Yuan, the Preparatory Office of the Central Land Administration, the Anti-Smuggling Department of the Ministry of Finance, the directly subordinate units, etc., for the 19th year. (3) The regulations for the collection of business tax in each province were submitted to the Economic and Financial Groups for review. (8th day Central News Agency dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Economic and Financial Groups of the Central Political Conference will review the business tax regulations of each province on the 14th. (8th day Central News Agency dispatch)

British Government

Has Yielded on Extraterritoriality 4

Only Wishes to Retain a Portion of Shanghai

(Nanjing) According to reliable external sources, the British government has yielded on the issue of extraterritoriality, agreeing to abandon it entirely except for retaining it in Shanghai. It is said that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs will respond within days. (8th day Special Dispatch)

Sichuan War Has Ceased 5

Two Lius to Meet in Jiangjin to Revise Agreement

(Nanjing) In Sichuan, the troops of Deng and Tian amount to no more than 60,000 men. Deng's troops are fewer. Liu Wenhui's troops are said to number 80,000, and Liu Xiang's troops are said to number 120,000. Liu Wenhui, persuaded by Liu Xiang, is expected not to align with Deng and Tian. The war has now ceased, and further action will be determined based on the outcome of the Jiangjin meeting. Today's Sichuan telegrams are as follows: (1) Chengdu, 8th day: Deng Xihou and Tian Songyao's original attack on Li Qixiang was first agreed upon by Liu Wenhui. Later, Liu Xiang repeatedly telegraphed Liu Wenhui, explaining the advantages and disadvantages and appealing to their uncle-nephew relationship, persuading him to lean towards the center and maintain peace. Liu's intention was slightly moved, so he remained in a wait-and-see attitude. Deng and Tian, knowing they were isolated, immediately stopped advancing and requested that the Chongqing army also stop advancing, etc. (2) Chengdu, 8th day: Liu Wenhui telegraphed Liu Xiang, inviting him to meet in Luzhou. Liu Xiang replied that as long as it is beneficial to the party and the country, he can go to the province, and it is not necessary to meet in Luzhou. Liu Wenhui changed the meeting place to Jiangjin, and it is expected to take place before the 15th. (3) Chengdu, 8th day: Yang Sen, when the Sichuan war was fierce, planned to lead his troops to advance towards Guang'an. Now, due to the ceasefire, he has changed to advancing towards Dazhou. (4) Chongqing, 7th day: As a result of this war, Liu Xiang's troops have expanded to the five counties of Wusheng, Dazu, Tongliang, Bishan, and Hechuan. Liu Wenhui incorporated the troops of Chen Hongwen and Chen Dingmian and occupied the two counties of Huayang and Jianyang. (8th day)

(Chongqing) After Liu Xiang of Chongqing ordered the forward troops to stop attacking, Tian Songyao also telegraphed the troops stationed in Shunqing from the province to temporarily stop advancing. The two Lius decided to change the meeting place to Jiangjin to discuss methods to maintain peace in Sichuan, and the Sichuan war may be resolved peacefully. (7th day Central News Agency dispatch)

Sino-Turkish Commercial Treaty Conference 6

Turkish Delegate Arrived in Nanjing Yesterday

(Nanjing) The Turkish response to the Sino-Turkish Commercial Treaty has been reviewed by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and Turkish Delegate Forde was telegraphed to come to Nanjing for consultation. The Turkish Delegate arrived in Nanjing on the 8th with two counselors. At 4:00 PM, a meeting was held at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. The Chinese side was represented by Li Jinlun and Hu Shize. The Chinese side raised the points of disagreement with the Turkish response, mainly regarding the treatment of overseas Chinese and customs taxation. After detailed discussions by both sides, the Chinese side submitted a response, requesting the Turkish Delegate to forward it to his government for review. (8th day Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) Li Mingzhong led all the personnel of the Governor's Office at 8:00 AM on the 8th, taking a special train on the Pinghan Railway north to Xinyang and then to Huangchuan. A communication office was established in Hankou, and Director Lu of the 22nd Route Army Office concurrently handled rear affairs. Li told people before his departure that he would issue a general offensive order as soon as the arrangements in Huangchuan were completed, and would eliminate the Red bandits in the border area of the three provinces before May 5th. Second Bandit Suppression Propaganda Office

All Personnel Sworn In 9

(Nanjing) All personnel of the Second Bandit Suppression Propaganda Office, led by Chiang Chien-jen, went to Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Mausoleum on the morning of the 8th for an oath-taking ceremony. Liu Lu-yin was appointed by the Central Government to administer the oath and deliver a speech. Chiang Chien-jen then gave a reply and dispersed. Printing of New Stamps 10

(Nanjing) A certain senior official of the Ministry of Communications said that stamps were previously printed by the Printing Bureau of the Ministry of Finance. However, the portrait of Chairman Chiang on the previous Unified Commemorative Stamps was distorted. This time, the new stamps use the portraits of Dr. Sun Yat-sen and martyrs. After several revisions of the plate, the workmanship was still lacking, so the portrait of Dr. Sun Yat-sen was handed over to a British merchant to print, and the remaining plates were made in Britain and still printed by the Printing Bureau. The value is only 200,000, and the rumor of a loss of 5 million is inaccurate. (8th day Central News Agency dispatch)

Central Land Administration 11

Preparations in Two Phases

(Nanjing) Wu Shang-ying, director of the Preparatory Office of the Central Land Administration, will prepare various implementation plans and technical solutions in two phases. The first phase is to investigate the actual situation and customary practices of land administration in various localities, and to compile statistics on the general land prices of each province, the achievements of previous land surveys, and to study the established rules of land administration in various countries, and to draft various auxiliary regulations for the Land Law, and land registration procedures. Regarding the internal organization of the office, one director will be appointed to administer the affairs of the entire office and direct and supervise subordinate officials under the order of the Executive Yuan. Two secretaries will be appointed, and five groups will be established: general affairs, surveying design, registration design, valuation design, and administrative design. The monthly expenses are about 8,000 yuan. It has been submitted to the National Government for approval and implementation, and it has been ordered to be directly under the Executive Yuan in accordance with Article 27 of the Land Law. However, the director previously planned to hire the Englishman Lu Wenze as a surveying technology specialist. Chairman Chiang instructed that, due to insufficient funds, economy should be given priority, and Lu Wenze could be postponed if he had not been hired. The office has informed the future and will postpone the discussion. (8th day Special Dispatch)

Hebei Party Reorganization Committee

Wang Shuchang and Others Take Office 14

(Beiping) Wang Shuchang, Ma Yuchen, and He Yufang of the Hebei Reorganization Committee took office at the Provincial Party Headquarters at 11:00 AM today. More than 100 people attended, including Zhang Ji, Chu Minyi, Yu Xuezhong, Zhang Xueming, Hu Ruoyu, Bao Yulin, and Jing Youyan. Zhang Ji administered the oath and delivered a speech, saying that there were many mistakes in Hebei party affairs last year. The Central Government hopes that the three comrades will enable party-government cooperation in Hebei, avoid many disputes, and enable the party's principles to proceed smoothly. He hopes that all comrades will take fairness as their psychology, lead the people to jump into the people, make the people partified, and especially hope that the county governments will assist the party affairs to carry out the party's seven movements. Wang Shuchang replied that he would respectfully accept the instructions of Chairman Zhang and cooperate and assist each other in party-government affairs from now on. (8th day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Yu Xuezhong told reporters that he will take office as the Reorganization Committee of the Municipal Government on the 13th, with Zhang Ji administering the oath. The date of Deputy Commander Zhang's arrival in Beiping is not yet determined. The Deputy Ministry has sent personnel to Beiping to prepare the location, which has not yet been determined between the old Ministry of Foreign Affairs or the old Ministry of Communications. (8th day Special Dispatch)

Liaoning Diplomatic Association 16

Passes Five Important Resolutions

(Shenyang) The Liaoning National Diplomatic Association held a joint meeting at the Shenyang YMCA from the 5th to the 8th. The opening ceremony was held on the morning of the 5th, with two discussion meetings and one lecture on diplomatic common sense each day. Chairman of the Congress Yan Yuheng announced five resolutions for the three days: (A) The case of redeeming the Chinese Eastern Railway: (1) Telegrammed Mo Dehui, urging him to fight to the death at the conference table to achieve the goal of redeeming the Chinese Eastern Railway, otherwise, he should return home and not humiliate the people's lives. (2) Telegrammed the whole country, advocating the immediate redemption of the Chinese Eastern Railway. (3) Telegraphed various countries to declare the reasons for redeeming the Chinese Eastern Railway. (4) Declared to the Soviet government and the people, requesting them to return the Chinese Eastern Railway based on the declarations of 1919 and 1920, and to take into account international credibility. (5) Organized a committee to redeem the Chinese Eastern Railway, with three departments for investigation, funding, and evaluation. (B) Resolutions on the case of immigration to solidify the border: (1) Encourage compatriots in the interior to move to the Northeast. (2) The actual situation in the Northeast is not known to compatriots in the interior, and the government and various provincial legal groups should be requested to jointly organize propaganda agencies to lead the immigration. (3) Local governments and legal groups should earnestly treat refugees coming to the Northeast and try to settle them so that they can live in peace. (4) Request the Chinese Red Cross and the Red Swastika Society to pay special attention to the relief of immigrants in the Northeast and allocate large amounts of funds for application. (5) Request various transportation agencies to give refugees special treatment. (6) Educational authorities in each province should set up special disciplines for immigrants to establish a foundation for loving and protecting the Northeast. (7) Promote agricultural cooperation and propaganda movements. (8) Suppress bandits to protect farmers. (9) Jointly organize Northeast immigration groups by the people of the Northeast for the convenience of compatriots in the interior. (C) Resolutions on the case of abolishing consular jurisdiction: (1) Telegraph the National Government to take decisive measures to unconditionally and immediately recover consular jurisdiction. (2) Expand the propaganda movement to abolish consular jurisdiction and urge the government to take decisive measures quickly. (D) There should be full preparations before resuming trade and diplomatic relations with Russia, resolutions: (1) Telegram to the national people to pay attention to: (1) Russian anti-propaganda, (2) Obstructing the development of domestic industry in many ways, (3) Conspiracy to undermine social order and disrupt law and order. (2) Please Central Party Headquarters, Ministry of Industry, Northeast Political Affairs Committee, provincial party headquarters and industrial groups organize large-scale industrial joint management methods. (3) The diplomatic association should start from the elementary and middle school level and provide appropriate educational materials: (1) The history of Sino-Russian negotiations, so that they know the Russian conspiracy and cannot be pleased by its sweet words, (2) Recite the facts of the Red Disaster in Guangdong, Hunan and Jiangxi, so that they know that the Communist disaster is like a flood. (3) Do your best to publicize the Three People's Principles to enrich the children's hearts and avoid the invasion of the Red Imperialism. (E) Resolutions on the South Manchurian Railway issue: (1) Promote Northeast commerce and industry. (2) Build a Northeast railway network. (3) Delegates from the Northeast attending the National Conference entrusted by the General Assembly will propose to negotiate the recovery of the South Manchurian Railway and its affiliated land. (8th day Central News Agency dispatch)

Yang's Troops Stationed in Fenyang 17

Chou Zengyi Succeeds as Director of Finance

(Taiyuan) Shang Zhen told reporters that it was purely a misunderstanding that the troops stationed in the two sides of Fenyang prevented the Jin army from entering the country. Song Zheyuan and Feng Zhi'an telegraphed orders to stop it, and the situation has eased. The Dongguan barracks have been vacated to prepare for Yang's troops to station. Yang's troops are now in Qixian Yangwu Town, shrinking into a group, under the command of Zhao Xiezong. The Northeast inspection committee has gone to inspect, and after the inspection, they will depart for Fenyang. I have telegraphed the details of the past to the various armies, and there will never be any more problems. The reporter asked what will happen to Feng's future post. Shang replied that this is another matter. The Central Government and the Northeast both hope that he will go abroad as soon as possible. I and Mingxuan and others also share this view. Finally, the reporters requested the cancellation of press censorship, and Shang agreed to notify the telegraph bureau to cancel it from today. (8th day Special Dispatch)

Tianjin Waterworks Strike

Mediation Faces Obstacles 18

(Tianjin) Through the mediation of the Municipal Government, the Public Security Bureau, and the Social Affairs Bureau, the company has acknowledged all twelve conditions proposed by the workers in the waterworks strike, except for a slight change in the salary increase. The company agrees to the following salary increases: 30% for monthly salaries of one to fifteen yuan; 20% for monthly salaries of fifteen to thirty yuan; monthly salaries of 31 to 35 yuan will be paid a uniform 37.5 yuan. The Municipal Government persuaded the workers to make concessions. The union held a members' meeting on the morning of the 8th, resolving to accept the Municipal Government's mediation. The agreement could have been signed and work resumed in the afternoon. However, in the afternoon, the company raised questions to the Municipal Government, saying that the central government promulgated the Trade Union Law, which should be based on workers, and that the Ji'an Waterworks Union not only has employees of the company as members, but also several directors and supervisors of the union are employees. Such unions that do not conform to the Trade Union Law are difficult to recognize. Therefore, the official mediation has completely broken down. The Municipal Government is afraid that the strike will expand and has scheduled to continue mediation on the 9th. (8th day Special Dispatch)

Current Commentary

Britain Invites German Dignitaries to London 22

The British government invited the German Prime Minister and Foreign Minister to Britain for a meeting. European countries are now paying great attention to this. Originally, what Britain invited was not just Germany alone. Although France did not agree to go, it did not refuse. In Italy, it is said that it is also on the list of invitations. However, due to the different situations in various countries, there are different views on the invitation. Germany's intention is that, at a time when discussions on the German-Austrian tax agreement are in full swing, Britain has neither expressed fierce opposition nor taken this action of inviting a meeting, which is diplomatically beneficial and harmless. Therefore, there is unanimous and enthusiastic welcome from all parties in the country. The Berlin Daily even considers it a sign of Anglo-German cooperation after the European War. Its approval of this move is conceivable.

Since the European War, the international union has had almost a fixed pattern, but only a few victorious powers have distributed it to each other, and the rest of the countries have obeyed their orders. There is no so-called diplomacy, let alone the strategy of vertical and horizontal integration. Since last year, Germany has gradually shown its prominence in the League of Nations and won the reputation of various countries. Until recently, there has been the development of the German-Austrian tax agreement, which has opened up a new situation in the stagnant international situation. Now, there is also the informal gathering between Britain and Germany. The diplomatic situation in Europe may change because of this. It is appropriate for various countries to pay serious attention to it.

Initial Draft of People's Assembly Organization Law Amended 39

(Nanjing) A certain Central Committee member said that the initial draft of the National Assembly Organization Law originally included a clause stating that proposals that violate the Party Program and superstitions should not be included on the agenda. This was deemed redundant and has now been deleted, because proposals must go through review, and whether or not they should be included on the agenda is the responsibility of the reviewers. Proposals that violate the Party Program and superstitions naturally cannot be put to a vote, so there is no need to create a separate clause. Furthermore, it is believed that the National Assembly should first resolve that the capital be permanently located in Nanjing. Some committee members advocate including this in the Provisional Constitution. (8th, Special Dispatch)

Reorganization of Hai River Public Bonds 48

(Tianjin) The 4 million yuan for the reorganization of the Hai River public bonds used the 25% surcharge on customs duties as a principal repayment fund. It was planned to be issued last spring, but when military conflicts occurred between the North and the South, the central government feared that Xishan would divert the funds for military use and ordered the issuance to be stopped. However, the customs surcharge continued to be collected. By now, four drawings have been made for principal repayment, totaling 800,000 yuan. The Hai River Reorganization Committee recently borrowed 300,000 yuan from the fund with bond tickets worth 300,000 yuan. The remaining 2.9 million yuan has been approved by the central government for issuance. It is scheduled that Han Linsheng, Huang Zongfa, and Ye Jingxin will contact the banking community on the 9th and issue the bonds at 98% of their face value. However, the deposit of funds among the nine banks still needs to be discussed. (8th, Special Dispatch)

Truth About Sudden Rebellion on Portuguese Madeira Island 68

Not Attempting to Secede from Motherland

Only Seeking to Achieve Autonomy

Reuters, London, 7th A rebellion has broken out on Madeira Island (Portuguese territory west of Morocco). Although there is no news of fighting yet, the situation has changed. The Portuguese authorities are now rushing to send a cruiser, fully loaded with soldiers, guns, artillery, and aircraft, to the island. Rebels on the island are also gathering crowds to prepare to resist. There are many British tourists on the island, but news from London says that the rebels are not infringing on foreigners. As a precaution, the British government has dispatched the cruiser HMS London from Gibraltar to Funchal (the capital of Madeira Island). The cause of this rebellion is the residents' dissatisfaction with the reinstatement of the former civil administrator, Freitas.

Reuters, London, 7th According to a telegram from Lisbon, four Portuguese battalions, carrying war equipment and aircraft, have set out for Madeira Island. Colonel Borges has been appointed as the pacification commissioner.

National, Madrid, 8th Portuguese authorities are censoring mail and telegrams. Hence news that has reached the border cannot be verified. It is claimed that the Portuguese government is continuing to send troops to Funchal to quell the unrest. The contingent includes two battalions of infantry, one battalion of artillery, and one machine-gun battalion. They will be protected ashore by two cruisers and four naval aircraft previously deployed. It is apparent that the present troops on the island have acted in unison. Their objective is not to separate from Portugal, but to obtain autonomy. They will comply only with those Portuguese government orders that are constitutional.

Anglo-German Conference in London 69

A Preliminary Indication of Cooperation between the Two Countries

Date Still to be Agreed

France and Italy Invited to Participate Simultaneously

Briand Did Not Clearly Refuse

Reuters, Paris, 7th The proposed conference between British Foreign Secretary Henderson and German Chancellor Brüning and Foreign Minister Curtius in London is still a matter of general discussion. According to reliable sources, the British Foreign Secretary discussed the matter with French Foreign Minister Briand several weeks ago. Briand did not reject it, but has not yet replied, as he wishes to base his response on the needs of domestic policy. It is expected that other countries, especially Italy, will be invited to send representatives to the conference.

National, Berlin, 8th The date on which the German Chancellor and Foreign Minister will travel to England has not yet been agreed between the British and German governments. The proposed dates of May 1st and 8th are both problematic. The British government has suggested postponing it until the end of May, but the German side does not agree and wishes to meet before the meeting of the League of Nations Administrative Council. Therefore, the two sides are still discussing the date.

National, Paris, 7th The British government's invitation to politicians from France, Italy, and Germany to hold an informal gathering in London dates back to mid-February. This has now been confirmed by the French Ministry of Foreign Affairs through a semi-official French news agency. However, Briand did not immediately reject the invitation at the time, and has not yet replied. He has only stated that his ability to meet with British and German politicians at the villa of British Prime Minister Jixiers will depend on the progress of the drafting of the Naval Agreement. As for the Italian side, Prime Minister Mussolini may not be able to go to England, but Foreign Minister Grandi may go on his behalf. It has also been said that one of the main reasons for the French Foreign Minister's unwillingness to go to England is that Britain has long held sway in European diplomatic affairs. If he were to acquiesce to this situation, it would further increase Britain's prestige, which in the eyes of the French would inevitably have an impact on Briand's position.

National, Berlin, 7th German newspapers, regardless of their political affiliation, have expressed extreme pleasure at Chancellor Brüning and Foreign Minister Curtius accepting the British invitation. Although the British invitation was issued before the publication of the German-Austrian customs union, this kind of private gathering is even more important now than before, because the German-Austrian customs union issue is bound to take up an important part of the talks. The disarmament issue, reparations issues, and the Russian issue may be secondary. The Berlin Daily believes that the British government's invitation is an indication of the British willingness to join hands with the Germans again, while the German World News says that Brüning has always been unwilling to participate in diplomatic affairs. The fact that he has now given his approval to go to England must mean that he has a plan in mind to deal with the various problems in a spirit of friendship, in order to save Germany from its predicament and seek the common good. As for the various concerns of the British about the German-Austrian customs union, it will not be difficult to dispel them with this trip. The sincerity of the British politicians in initiating this move is highly admirable.

Germany Demands League of Nations Publish

The Real Situation of the Military Equipment of Various Countries 70

National, Geneva, 7th German Foreign Minister Curtius has sent a letter to the Secretary-General of the League of Nations, requesting that the current state of military equipment of the countries participating in next year's international disarmament conference be published. The letter has now been published, stating that the League of Nations Council, at its meeting in January, instructed Mr. de Romens to compile a report on the state of military equipment of various countries. Germany is of the opinion that it is impossible to publish a complete report without submitting the same set of questions to the governments of the countries concerned for answers, because it is not possible to compare the military equipment of various countries without using this method. The drafting of the questions to be asked should be included on the agenda of the Council meeting in May.

In short, the fate of the Hamaguchi cabinet is only a matter of time.

It seems that it was decided at that time to seek Wakatsuki's assistance. Therefore, Wakatsuki's actions from now on are worthy of attention, and it seems that Prime Minister Hamaguchi will express a major decision only after the party is united.

Activities of the Governor of the Bank of England in America 73

Seeking to Maintain London's Superior Position in the Market

Met with Hoover, Did Not Discuss Silver Issues

Reuter, Washington, 7th – Norman, the Governor of the Bank of England, visited U.S. President Hoover at the White House today. Although the content of the meeting was not disclosed, Norman stated to reporters upon leaving that the issue of silver was not mentioned.

Reuters, New York, 7th – The Governor of the Bank of England, Norman, spoke to leading figures in the American financial community today. According to the New York Times, Norman advocated that leaders of the U.S. Federal Reserve and European central banks should meet regularly. Although these meetings would not have binding effect, Norman cautioned that if American officials completely disregarded the situation in foreign countries, it would be shortsighted policy. Present at the meeting were Treasury Secretary Mellon and Federal Reserve Governor Meyer, among others. It is understood that the topics discussed were of a routine nature, involving international trade and finance. Reuters, Paris, 8th – A certain newspaper is paying close attention to Norman's activities in America, claiming that the main purpose of the Governor of the Bank of England's trip is to maintain the superior position of the London market in dominating international lending, and to seek British participation in the creation of an international banking consortium. It further stated that France still advocates that Britain and France should cooperate with each other on international financial issues based on shared interests, but France is not willing to undertake any attempt that would allow the consortium to dispose of France's cash without offering commercial benefits in return.

Associated Press, Reno, 7th – U.S. Senator Oddie declared today that his plan to travel to the Far East for investigation is ready. He will stay in China for two months to investigate the impact of the drastic fall in silver prices and collect opinions from Chinese experts on the silver market. The main purpose of this trip is to determine whether the United States can loan silver to China for currency reform purposes. Oddie is a Republican from Nevada, a state known for silver production. Therefore, Oddie and Pittman, a Democrat from the same state, are both paying close attention to stabilizing silver prices. They are the strongest advocates in the Senate for lending silver to China, to open up an outlet for silver mining and reduce stockpiles of silver.

Internal Split Among Local Red Bandits in Western Fujian

Fuzhou Correspondence: Red bandits on the Jiangxi border entered Chong'an and Jianning counties in Fujian Province a month ago, and were driven back by the brigades of Lin Bingzhou, Qian Yuguang, Liu Shangzhi, and Zhou Zhiqun. The remaining Red bandits in Jiangxi Province, due to Chiang Kwang-nai's troops advancing to Xingguo, have retreated from Guangchang and Ningdu to Shicheng and Ruijin. At the same time, scattered Red bandits have also invaded Jianning and Chong'an. Although the garrison troops have dispatched teams to suppress them, they have not been completely eliminated. It is heard that Chuan Bocui, the most senior figure among the western Fujian Red bandits from the Cancellation faction, believes that the failure was due to the improper command of the pseudo-Western Fujian Military Commission and has expressed resentment. Establishment of the Shanxi Financial Reorganization Committee 81

Taiyuan Correspondence: The Jin Province Financial Reorganization Design Committee held its inaugural meeting in the Provincial Government Conference Hall at 9:00 AM yesterday (the 3rd). Attendees included Provincial Government Chairman Shang Zhen, Provincial Government Committee Members Qiu Zengyi, Chang Bingyi, Feng Sizhi, Li Shangren, Guo Baoqing, Provincial Party Headquarters Representative Liu Huaiqi, 6th Army Commander Yang Aiyuan, 5th Army Chief of Staff Yang Fenglin, Results Office Military Supplies Group Leader Guo Dianping, Financial Reorganization Office Representative Yang Peiqiao, Chamber of Commerce Representative Wang Zhaotai, Money Industry Guild Representatives Hao Qingzhao and Duan Guozhen, Education Association Representative Yang Renkang, Provincial Bank Representatives Yan Yuqin, Li Buqing, Chang Yunwen, and specially appointed Committee Member Gao Hong, totaling nineteen people. Chairman Shang Zhen conducted the ceremony as usual. The chairman reported that recently the price of provincial currency has plummeted, rumors have arisen, prices have increased, and the people's lives have become increasingly difficult, especially for the working class. Military expenses have not yet been settled, and demobilization funds have not yet been allocated. Fearing social unrest due to popular sentiment, the reorganization of finance is the most urgent and pressing matter. The provincial government has an unshirkable responsibility for the reorganization of finance, but due to the magnitude of the matter and the urgency of the situation, it cannot be handled well without collective wisdom and effort. Therefore, I proposed at the provincial government meeting to establish a Financial Reorganization Design Committee, which was resolved to be organized by the provincial party headquarters, provincial government, army commanders, results office military supplies group, financial reorganization office, chamber of commerce, money industry guild, education association, farmers association, provincial bank, and financial experts. Ten measures were also passed, scheduled to take effect today. Hereafter, meetings will be held every Thursday morning. Temporary meetings may be held in the event of special financial incidents. This is the origin of the organization of this committee. Furthermore, the provincial government has long been paying attention to the reorganization of finance. The financial reorganization proposal was put forward for discussion at the first meeting. A resolution was passed to telegraph the central government, approving the restoration of financial public bonds. The central government has now submitted it to the Executive Yuan for review. The second temporary meeting of the Provincial Committee also resolved to telegraph the central government, urging prompt approval, and to telegraph Deputy Commander Zhang, urging the prompt allocation of demobilization funds and urging the central government to quickly approve the financial public bond measures. We have received a telegram from Deputy Commander Zhang, stating that the demobilization funds have been ordered to be remitted immediately, and the telegram urging the central government to approve the restoration of financial public bonds has also been sent on his behalf. However, whether the central government will approve the restoration of financial public bonds cannot be predicted. We must seek our own methods of relief and never sit idly by as finance collapses and society falls into chaos. From this point of view, this committee is even more necessary. In short, the significance of the organization of this committee lies in gathering collective wisdom and effort to seek a fundamental solution to the financial problems of this province in order to eliminate future disasters. I hope that representatives of various agencies and groups will express their insightful opinions as much as possible, so that the provincial government can adopt them. Then representatives of various agencies and groups successively expressed their opinions, and the meeting adjourned at 12:00 PM. Attached is the organization method of the committee: (Article 1) This committee will focus on studying fundamental methods for rescuing provincial currency and consolidating the financial foundation of this province, and is named the Financial Reorganization Design Committee. (Article 2) This committee is organized by the provincial party headquarters, provincial government, army commanders, results office military supplies group, financial reorganization office, chamber of commerce, money industry guild, education association, farmers association, provincial bank, and financial experts appointed by the provincial government. (Article 3) Each of the aforementioned agencies must send at least one person to attend. Each army commander may send a representative to attend. (Article 4) This committee is located within the provincial government. (Article 5) The meeting time for this committee is from 9:00 AM to 11:00 AM every Thursday morning, but temporary meetings may be convened by the provincial government in the event of special financial incidents. (Article 6) Each agency and each committee member may submit suggestions at any time. The review and arrangement of the suggestions will be handled by personnel appointed by the conference at any time. (Article 7) The resolutions of this committee may be suggested to the provincial government at any time. (Article 8) The personnel in charge of this committee's affairs and record-keeping may be temporarily transferred from various agencies. (Article 9) The committee members of this committee will not be paid, and the necessary office expenses within the committee will be allocated by the provincial government at any time. (Article 10) This method will be implemented from the date of resolution by the Provincial Government Committee.

Wu Tiecheng's Talk in Harbin 82

Inspects for Three Days Before Going to Heilongjiang

Harbin Correspondence: Wu Tiecheng, who is inspecting party affairs in the Northeast, arrived in Harbin from Jilin at 8:00 AM on April 1st. He plans to stay in Harbin for three days and go to Heilongjiang on the afternoon of the 7th. He also plans to stay in Heilongjiang for three days before returning to Liaoning, passing through Pingjin, and is scheduled to return to Beijing in late April. When Wu arrived in Harbin, leaders from all walks of life and key figures from various agencies went to the station to welcome him, making the situation very warm. Wu is currently staying at the headquarters of the Railway Protection Army Commander-in-Chief on Da Zhijie in Qinjiagang. Many dignitaries have been visiting him. On the same day, Wu spoke with reporters as follows: (Question) After the Northeast party affairs are made public, are there any diplomatic issues? (Answer) No problem. Chinese people run the Chinese party, and foreigners have no right to interfere. However, foreigners are unwilling and indeed very afraid of the establishment of party affairs. (Question) After the Harbin Municipal Party Headquarters is established, do Chinese employees of the East China Railway have to join the party? Because the East China Railway has diplomatic relations, the Soviet Union pays close attention to whether Chinese employees join the party. (Answer) This should be allowed to happen naturally, and there will be no coercion. However, we hope they will join the party. (Question) If Chinese employees of the East China Railway join the party, will they form another party headquarters? (Answer) It will also be managed by the local party headquarters and no separate party headquarters will be established. (Question) What are your opinions on Northeast party affairs? (Answer) I hope that each party headquarters will work hard in accordance with the two points of culture and propaganda. In addition, we will carry out seven tasks: afforestation, road construction, sanitation保甲, promotion of national goods. Because culture can improve the people's level, propaganda can make people aware of our party. Other general tasks, each party headquarters must implement. (Question) Will the central government send personnel to help the Northeast organize the party? (Answer) The central government will let the local government handle the Northeast party affairs and will not interfere, but hopes to proceed in accordance with the central government's guidelines. (Question) There are only three party members of the local committee in Harbin. Can the party headquarters be established? (Answer) It remains to be discussed and decided. I hope to see it accomplished before I leave Harbin. (Question) What are the measures for the masses to join the party? (Answer) For those who have not joined the party, a period of one year is set to prepare for party membership. (Question) What about officials? (Answer) Civil officials at the section chief level and military officers at the major level or above must join the party, but it is not certain, etc.

Wu is scheduled to give a public lecture on party affairs at the Wai Daoli Church at 4:00 PM on the 5th at the invitation of various groups. When the Harbin Municipal Party Headquarters is formally established within the Special Zone Administrative Office, a suitable location will be sought. Also, Party Committee Member Zou Shangyou has gone to Tianjin with Tianjin Mayor Zhang Xueming. It is heard that the vacant seat still needs to be filled by the central government. (April 4th)

Zhejiang Province Sends Personnel to Investigate Mineral Resources 83

Zhejiang Province's mineral products are numerous and diverse. Previously, the Mineral Resources Survey Office of the Construction Department investigated and found that there are more than twenty kinds of metals and non-metals, totaling more than two hundred locations. These include the gold mine in Kaihua, the lead and silver mines in Zhuji and Fuyang, the tin mines in Qingtian and Yongjia, the iron ore in Zhuji and Yuhang, and the iron ore in Changxing, Jiande, and Ninghai. Tin ore is mostly found in the upper reaches of the Xin'an River, and tin is mostly found in the Oujiang River basin. Non-metals such as coal and fluorite are the most common mineral products in Zhejiang Province. Coal is produced in the counties in the upper reaches of the Qujiang River, and there are also many coalfields in Changxing and Wuxing on the border of Anhui and Zhejiang. Fluorite mines are scattered like stars east of the Qiantang River and west of Mount Tiantai, numbering about fifty. Other minerals such as alum stone in Pingyang, agalmatolite in Qingtian and Songyang, and mica in Xiangshan are also very abundant. Currently, the office plans to send personnel to organize investigation teams to survey five areas in the province that have not been investigated but are considered to warrant further exploration. The first area is along the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, the second area is the Lingjiang River basin, the third area is the Oujiang River basin, the fourth area is the Feiyun River basin and coastal areas, and the fifth area is Wuxing, Changxing, and other counties. However, the survey routes in each area vary in length, and the survey period depends on the time required for the work, with the longest being three to five months and the shortest being about one month.

Wuhu Express News 84

The election of representatives to the National Assembly in Wuhu County has commenced today for the party departments and district branches. Voting is scheduled to be completed before the 9th. The County Party Department held a special meeting yesterday to resolve to appoint Zhang Shuye, Li Tangbi, Geng Xidao, Gu Wuwei, Chen Zuoshan, Pan Yunkun, Huang Shuhan, Huang Huaili, Qi Yigan, and Wu Jixin, a total of ten people, as election supervisors in various districts for the National Assembly election.

According to a secret report, a Communist Party organization is operating in Wuhu, hiding important Communist Party members. Yesterday, the provincial authorities specially dispatched Zhang to Wuhu to work with the Public Security Bureau to select police officers to arrest nine suspects last night, including a woman surnamed Du. Four people have already been sent to the province today.

During the military period, when the army passed through Wuhu, a military reception center was jointly established by the Public Security Bureau, the County Government, and the General Chamber of Commerce to facilitate hospitality. Recently, the County Chamber of Commerce was reorganized. Due to the high costs of the center, in addition to collecting an additional 6,200 yuan from land taxes, the General Chamber of Commerce has contributed more than 17,200 yuan. It is difficult to maintain this in the long run. It was proposed to close the center immediately, but Magistrate Yu was concerned that Wuhu Port was a vital waterway and that the center should not be closed until the military situation was resolved. In addition to petitioning the Finance Department to approve the continued collection of a one-cent per mu donation, he also ordered the County Chamber of Commerce to continue operating the center.

The Civil Affairs Department instructed the Wuhu County Government to prepare for the establishment of the Wuhu Relief Home. Magistrate Yu, after receiving the order, immediately appointed Wu Xingzhou, chairman of the County Chamber of Commerce, to concurrently serve as the president of the home, and Tao Yutang as the vice president, and began preparations. (7th)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 85

List of Agricultural and Educational Association Members Submitted to Province for Review: The County Election Supervisor, Jin Qingzhang, telegraphed various educational and agricultural associations on the 6th, stating that the County Reorganization Committee's letter had been approved. The Provincial Reorganization Committee instructed that the lists of participants in the county agricultural associations' elections should be based on the lists of representatives of the established township agricultural associations. The educational associations could also submit the lists of members of the established district educational associations. All submissions were to be sent to the province by April 8th. The Provincial General Supervisor, Yu, also telegraphed, instructing that all established district agricultural associations in the county should participate in the election. It was noted that the election of national representatives should be conducted in accordance with Article 7 of the Election Implementation Law. Due to the tight deadline, preparations might not be completed in time. After discussing with Standing Committee member Wang, it was decided that the County Party Reorganization Committee would provide written proof of the establishment of the district agricultural and educational associations, and the County Government would organize the previously submitted lists of associations, or rewrite the lists, and submit them together first. This was an expedient measure, and it was difficult to predict whether the province would recognize it as valid. It was reported that the lists of the educational associations of the first, third, fourth, fifth, and sixth districts, and the district agricultural associations of the seventh, eighth, ninth, and tenth districts, were sent to the Provincial Election General Office in Zhenjiang by Commissioner Liu Nailai by train on the evening of the 7th for review.

Command Headquarters Offers Rewards for the Capture of Bandits: Cao Pang, the commander of the bandit suppression in Songjiang, Jinshan, Pinghu, and Jiashan counties, is actively suppressing bandits in the hope of eliminating harm to the people and pacifying the region. Although the bandit leaders Tai Bao A Shu and Zhu Luo A Mei have been captured one after another, the remaining bandits are scattered in various directions and should be arrested with graded rewards in order to achieve complete success. The rewards are as follows: Tai Bao A Shu: 2,000 yuan; Zhu Luo A Mei: 1,000 yuan; Zhang Tongsheng, Zhao Guomin, and Lu Yaosheng: 800 yuan each; Tao Hulong, Xu Ajin (i.e., tailor Ajin), Yan Shushen, Weng Mingzhe, Li Wenjun, and Gu Peizhang: 500 yuan each; Xia Zexian, Xu Fusheng, Pan Amu, Liu Dexing, He Yinyu, and Yang Meimei: 300 yuan each; Yang Amei, Gu Along, Luo Heshang, Dai Kechang, Song Ziqing, Jin Jinhuo, Xue Song A'er, Shen Junsheng, and Dao Ming: 200 yuan each. This reward money is stored in the reserve banks of each county and managed by a management committee. Anyone who captures the above-mentioned bandits can collect the reward from the committee.

Officials and Gentry Telegraph Request for Execution of Bandit Leaders: Since Tai Bao A Shu and Zhu Luo A Mei were captured one after another, the people are rejoicing. Now, the four counties' public security fee management committee and the district offices have telegraphed to Provincial Chairman Ye and Director Zhang of the Pacification Office and Director Hu of the Civil Affairs Department, stating that Tai Bao A Shu and Zhu Luo A Mei have committed heinous crimes and have been arrested, which the people are celebrating. They earnestly request that they be executed on the spot without delay, lest accidents occur. Furthermore, Jinshan County Magistrate Huang Zhewen also telegraphed to his superiors, stating that the bandit leaders in Punan, Xu Tianxiong, nicknamed Tai Bao A Shu, and Wang Qiming, nicknamed Zhu Luo A Mei, colluded to rob and murder, committing notorious crimes. The county magistrate led the group police and consulted with the garrison troops to repeatedly search and suppress them. The bandit leaders disguised themselves and fled. Rewards were offered for their arrest. Recently, Xu Pucheng, the first district chief of the water police, and Fan Guozhong, the captain, discovered and arrested the bandit leaders in Shanghai. They earnestly request that orders be given to the relevant military police to execute them immediately to serve as a warning and to comply with public sentiment.

Suzhou 86

Results of the Wuxian National Assembly Election Announced: Wuxian County held elections for representatives to the National Assembly. The voting for the industrial and commercial groups was held on the 7th. The ballots were counted yesterday (8th) under the supervision of Supervisor Huang. According to the results of the ballot counting, Cheng Ganqing and Yu Xiaochuan each received 198 votes in the Chamber of Commerce, Qian Sunqing received 189 votes, Wang Jingting received 124 votes, Lan Bohua received 153 votes, and Shi Yunqing received 122 votes. The next highest votes were Hu Yuzhang with 78 votes and Jiang Kesheng with 68 votes. In the labor union, Xu Wensheng, Xia Xuejun, Zhao Xiangqin, Ding Xinfu, Lu Jupo, Ye Gui, and Qi Yonghao received the most votes.

Liuye Assessor Accused: Liuye Assessor has recently been accused by Qian Xinpei of collusion with the local tyrant Li Fenglai in covering up cases and asking for investigation. After receiving the report, the Higher Court ordered the county magistrate to investigate and verify the matter.

Young Man and Woman Commit Suicide by Poisoning Simultaneously: A sensational case of double suicide occurred at the Dadong Inn outside Suzhou. Both the man and woman are dead. On the 5th, a male and female traveler arrived at the inn and stayed in room 138 on the third floor. Both spoke with a Yangzhou accent. The woman was beautiful, and the man was also well-dressed. The man claimed to be Shuang Dewei, 30 years old, from Shanghai academia. On the 6th, they moved to room 93 downstairs because they felt the third floor was noisy. Before going to bed, they instructed the tea room to not wake them up early the next day. At 5 p.m. on the 7th, the tea room pushed open the door to check and found that both had taken poison and were dying and unable to speak. The two were lying side by side. The man stretched out his left arm and pillowed the woman's neck, and stretched his right foot over the woman's body. The inn hired Dr. Gu Suyu from Western medicine to examine them, but it was too late. They died shortly after. Yesterday morning (8th), the local court sent prosecutor Lai Gan to investigate. The man was wearing a gray cotton-padded jacket and pants, lined with a velvet shirt and a velvet cloth shirt. Besides a handkerchief, there was nothing else on him. The woman was wearing a gray woolen cheongsam with black trim, a pink cotton-padded jacket, jade-colored embroidered socks, and patent leather shoes. She had a gold chain around her neck with a gold medallion from the Tianbao Silver Shop in Hangzhou, three gold buttons, a Parker fountain pen, a gold watch on her left hand, a double-strand gold bracelet, and two jade rings on her fingers. There was a stamp box on the table in front of the bed, as well as 45 yuan in banknotes, two small foreign coins, and two white tin-packaged cigarettes. It was determined that both had died from poisoning and there was a suicide note, which roughly said: "We are committing suicide because we both have incurable diseases. There is no other reason, and it has nothing to do with this inn. We still have 45 yuan in banknotes, a gold bracelet, two gold rings, a fountain pen, a watch, two quilts, and some clothes. If a kind person would use the remaining money to arrange a thin coffin for burial, we would be very grateful."

Wuxi 87

Small Steamboat and Tugboat Nearly Sink: The Hengyu small steamboat of the China Steamship Company runs daily from Wuxi to Zhou Tieqiao, Yixing, and its business is very good. The morning before yesterday, the steamboat was towing a tugboat carrying seventy or eighty passengers when it departed from Wuxi. After 11 o'clock, when passing the Qianqiao Town pier, more than ten miles away from the city, it was about to dock when the Heqiao steamboat of the Zhixing Company came from the countryside to the city. As the two ships gave way to each other, the China tugboat suddenly hit a reef and the hull sank. The male and female passengers were all terrified, grabbing things and making an enormous mess. The sound of crying could be heard from far and wide. Fortunately, the tugboat had gradually approached the shore at this time, and the passengers were able to get ashore without drowning. However, all the luggage was submerged in the water, resulting in irreparable losses. The Rape of Maidservant Case Has Been Judged: Hu Nianzu, a male servant of Zhou Zhaofu, a wealthy merchant in Zhouxin Town in the third district of the county, raped a maidservant, Juxiang, who was under the age of sixteen. Zhou sent a representative, Lu Shilun, to report to the county court, and after repeated interrogations, Hu was detained. The prosecutor's office concluded its investigation the other day and filed a public prosecution with the same-level criminal court. The court president Yang held a trial and appointed lawyer Tang Ying as the pro bono defense attorney. The result of the trial was that Hu Nianzu was ordered to be returned to custody, and Juxiang was ordered to return home. Yesterday was the day for the verdict in this case. Judge Jin signed and brought Hu Nianzu to the court and sentenced him to three years and six months of imprisonment.

Outbreak of Meningitis Spreads in Urban and Rural Areas: The weather in the county has been unfavorable recently, causing widespread outbreaks of smallpox, measles, colds, and other illnesses, which have persisted for a long time. In addition, there is also meningitis. The hospitals in the urban area are receiving patients for treatment every day, and the situation is even more severe in rural areas. In the fifth district of the county, in the area around Gu Ting Temple in Maqi Township, there are many patients and deaths are occurring one after another. According to doctors, this dangerous illness will disappear as soon as the weather warms up.

The Strange Case of Beating a Model Cleared Up: Sun Shuruo, a resident of Nanjing Bridge in the city, bought a Henan girl named Xiaoqing as a maidservant in 1920. The girl is now of marriageable age and has a pleasing appearance. Therefore, Sun and his wife, Bao, loved and cherished her very much, treating her like their own daughter. On the 1st of this month, Xiaoqing suddenly contracted meningitis. Despite repeated medical treatments and visits to Puren Hospital, she eventually died due to the severity of the illness. Sun Shuruo then bought a coffin and temporarily placed it in the mulberry field in the backyard. However, on the 6th, the Dao Bao newspaper suddenly published a news item titled "Beating a Model," with the sub-headline "A Beautiful Maidservant Is Often Whipped, Covered in Wounds, and Inevitably Dies." It stated that "Sun Xiaoqing, the maidservant of the Sun family, was whipped dozens of times by Sun's wife, Bao, causing her to be seriously injured and unable to get out of bed, and she died on the second day." After seeing the report, Zhou Erkai, the chief prosecutor of the county court, immediately filed a case according to law because it concerned human life, and summoned the Sun couple to the court for investigation. After questioning them, he could not find any clues, so he summoned Wang Yongtai, the head of the Tu Tu, for questioning. Wang forcefully claimed that Xiaoqing had died of illness and that there was no abuse. Chief Prosecutor Zhou was afraid that there were other circumstances, so he immediately took the coroner, the clerk, and the bailiffs and accompanied Sun Shuruo to the graveyard to open the coffin for examination. Sun Shuruo then requested to be exempted from the examination and said that if the examination revealed any wounds, he would be willing to accept punishment, and if there were no wounds, he must investigate thoroughly. Chief Zhou did not allow it and immediately opened the coffin. After repeated examinations for a long time, there were no wounds on any part of the body. There were only a few blisters on the legs. Chief Prosecutor Zhou verified that there was no mistake and immediately ordered Sun Shuruo to re-coffin and return to the court. The Bao family was released after being brought to court for no reason and suffering this strange injustice, causing the dead to turn over in the coffin. She refused to leave and cried all the way home after being persuaded by others.

Zhenjiang 88

Three Women Kidnapped While Gathering Firewood: Wang, Jin, and Yang, villagers in Tanggang, western township, were kidnapped by bandits while gathering firewood. As the three women lived in the same village, they went to Wulong Mountain to gather firewood at 2 PM the other day. Unexpectedly, several bandits appeared in the mountain depression and kidnapped the three women. When the families of the three women did not see them return in the evening, they sent people to search the mountain, but there was no trace of them. Later, they inquired with nearby residents and learned that they had been kidnapped by bandits. The three families were very anxious and have sent people to search for their whereabouts.

The participants included the goldsmith guild, the porter's union, the machinist's union, the match worker's union, the silk reeling worker's union, the tile and lumber worker's union, the tin and shearing worker's union, the garment worker's union, the lumber hook-up guild, the hotel and hospitality worker's union, the musician's union, the thread making worker's union, the incense worker's union, and the tin and tobacco worker's union, for a total of fourteen unions.
