Important News

Minutes of the Jiangsu Provincial Higher General Qualification Examination Committee Meeting 175

The first meeting of the Jiangsu Provincial Higher General Qualification Examination Committee was held on April 6th at the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education. The committee members present were Hu Huanyong, Zhou Guangzhuo, Hu Pu’an, Liu Yizheng, Hu Dunfu, Chen Yuguang, Wu Yuandi, Wu Ruinian, Yan Fang, Xiang Shaoxuan, Yu Qingtang, and Chen Hexian. Chen Hexian chaired the meeting, and Han Shoujin served as the recorder. (Reported Matters): (1) The Examination Yuan sent a letter concerning the regulations, requiring the establishment of the Higher General Qualification Examination Committee before April 1st. (2) This committee hired members and began using its official seal on March 27th, reporting its establishment. (3) The Examination and Selection Committee issued an order stating that the Higher Qualification Examination dates, previously submitted and approved, would be from April 1st to the end of June this year. This meeting resolved that the General Qualification Examination would also be held between April 1st and the end of June this year. (4) The Examination and Selection Committee telegraphed regarding the registration and all procedures for the examination, which must be completed and reported between April 1st and the end of June. (Matters for Discussion): (1) Draft of the Committee's Detailed Rules of Procedure: Resolved to amend and pass. (2) Draft of the Rules of the Jiangsu Provincial Higher General Qualification Examination Office: Resolved to amend and pass. (3) Draft of the Jiangsu Provincial Higher General Qualification Examination Proctoring Rules: Resolved to amend and pass. (4) Draft of the Jiangsu Provincial Higher General Qualification Examination Venue Rules: Resolved to amend and pass. (5) Examination Dates: Resolved that May 17th would be the starting date for the Higher Qualification Examination and May 31st would be the starting date for the General Qualification Examination. (6) Registration Dates and Registration Fee Amount: Resolved that the registration period for both types of qualification examinations would be from April 10th to May 10th, with a registration fee of two yuan for each. (7) Resolved that applicants must have a guarantor who is a civil servant above the level of appointee in this province or a faculty member of a secondary school or above. (8) Resolved that Jiaoshan would be the location for grading the examination papers. (9) Resolved to appoint Han Shoujin as the director of the Qualification Examination Office. The meeting adjourned at 5:50 PM.

Proctoring Rules for Qualification Examinations

Article 1: These rules are formulated in accordance with Articles 10 and 11 of the Detailed Rules of Procedure of the Jiangsu Provincial Higher General Qualification Examination Committee. Article 2: Proctoring matters for the Jiangsu Provincial Higher General Qualification Examination shall be handled by proctoring committee members and invigilators in accordance with these rules. Article 3: Proctoring committee members shall be present at the examination venue during the examination, and invigilators shall enter the venue on time and assist in supervision under the direction of the proctoring committee members. Article 4: Proctoring committee members and invigilators shall manage the following matters in the examination venue: (1) Maintaining order in the examination venue. (2) Verifying photographs and checking seat numbers. (3) Distributing examination papers. (4) Collecting examination papers. (5) Other matters that may arise temporarily. Article 5: If examination fraud, violations of examination venue rules, or other irregular conduct are discovered in the examination venue, the proctoring committee members shall, depending on the circumstances, report the matter, order the person to leave the venue, or take other appropriate measures. If invigilators discover the aforementioned circumstances, they shall immediately stop the behavior or report it to the proctoring committee member for disposition, depending on the severity of the situation. Article 6: The remaining examination papers shall be temporarily kept by the proctoring committee member and handed over to the Qualification Examination Office for safekeeping after the end of the examination. Article 7: When collecting the examination papers, the proctoring committee member shall supervise the invigilators in removing the name slips and, after collecting all the papers, the proctoring committee member shall count and seal them for submission to the Qualification Examination Committee. Article 8: These rules shall be implemented after being approved by the Qualification Examination Committee and reported to the Examination and Selection Committee and the Jiangsu Provincial Government for record.

Order from the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education to Participate in the Shanghai Municipal

First Joint Sports Meet for Secondary Schools 177

—Three Days, April 24th to 26th—

The Long-Distance Race Will Be Held at 10 AM on the Morning of April 19th

Order from the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education to all municipal and private secondary schools that have been registered, are undergoing trial implementation, or are undergoing reform: In order to promote sports among the secondary schools in this city and among all citizens of the city, this bureau has scheduled the First Joint Sports Meet for Secondary Schools in Shanghai and a long-distance race, and has formulated competition rules and race rules, respectively, which have been submitted to the Municipal Government. Instruction No. 9698 stated, "All submitted documents are understood and approved. This bureau is ordered to publish and implement them separately. This order, document retained, etc." In compliance with this, publication and implementation are required. In addition to separate official letters, a copy of the competition rules and race rules are attached for your information. This order includes attached copies of the competition rules and race rules.

Rules of the First Shanghai Municipal Long-Distance Race

Article 1: The purpose of this association is to promote physical fitness among all citizens of the city.

Article 2: Any citizen of this city who is 16 years of age or older, except those whose profession is sports, may participate in the competition.

Article 3: The race route of this association is two laps around the streetcar line on the three roads of the Nanshi district, totaling 11,000 meters.

Article 4: This association will hold the competition at 10 AM on the morning of April 19th.

Article 5: This association will have one president, one secretary-general, one chief referee, and several counters, judges, and clerks to handle all matters.

Article 6: During the competition, each athlete shall proceed completely according to the route set by this association. If an athlete runs the wrong route, he/she shall return to the original wrong point and re-run. They shall not step onto the sidewalk, ask for help, or obstruct other athletes.

Article 7: Each athlete may request one guide to lead, but only those riding bicycles are allowed. (Guides may only start guiding athletes when they reach Xiaonanmen.)

Article 8: The number of winning athletes is fixed at 15. Those who finish the entire course within one hour, even if they are not in the top 15, will also be given commemorative items.

Article 9: The competition affairs shall be presided over by the chief referee. All decisions of the chief referee shall not be protested by the athletes.

Article 10: These rules shall be implemented after being approved and promulgated by the Municipal Bureau of Education and submitted to the Municipal Government for record.

Competition Regulations for the First Shanghai Municipal Joint Sports Meet for Secondary Schools 178

Article 1: This association is organized by the Municipal Bureau of Education for the purpose of promoting sports in all secondary schools in the city.

Article 2: All public and private registered secondary schools in the city may select students to be athletes for this association. Private secondary schools that have been approved by the Municipal Bureau of Education for trial implementation or reform may, with the approval of the Municipal Bureau of Education, select students to be athletes for this association.

Article 3: The venue for this association will be the track and field stadium of the Chinese National Sports Association on Route Père Robert.

Article 4: The opening date of this association is from April 24th to April 26th, 20th year. If necessary, the president of this association may decide to change it.

Article 5: This association shall have one president, one vice president, and one director of association affairs to preside over all association affairs.

Article 6: The association affairs of this association are divided into two departments: administrative and competitive. Each department has one director. The administrative department is divided into six sections: general affairs, accounting, documentation, editing, reception, and discipline. The competitive department is divided into two sections: competition and venue. The number of staff members in each section shall be determined by the director of association affairs based on the complexity of the affairs, and shall be hired by the president.

Article 7: The athletes' competition is divided into male and female categories. The events are as follows: (A) Men's Category: "Field Events" High jump, long jump, pole vault, triple jump, discus throw, javelin throw, shot put (12 pounds). "Track Events" 100 meters, 200 meters, 400 meters, 800 meters, 1500 meters, 5000 meters, 110-meter hurdles, 400-meter hurdles, 800-meter relay race, 1600-meter relay race. (B) Women's Category: "Field Events" High jump, long jump, javelin throw, shot put (8 pounds). "Track Events" 50 meters, 100 meters, 200 meters, 400-meter relay race.

Article 8: Each athlete's registration is limited to four events for men and three events for women, excluding relay races. Each school is limited to four people per department per event.

Article 9: The competition rules shall be handled in accordance with the competition rules of the Chinese National Sports Association.

Article 10: This association's championship trophies are divided into four types: men's team, women's team, men's individual, and women's individual.

(1) Team Championship: Awarded to the school with the most points. If two or more schools have the same score, the school with the most first-place finishes wins.

(2) Individual Championship: Awarded to the athlete with the most points. If two or more athletes have the same score, the athlete with the most first-place finishes wins.

Article 11: These regulations shall be implemented after being approved by the Municipal Bureau of Education and submitted to the Municipal Government for approval.

Free Talk

World Snippets 179

—Hai Ke

▲ In Amsterdam, the capital of the Netherlands, there are several windy street corners that are very cold in winter. Therefore, the municipal authorities have installed a kind of board in the underground of the police sentry posts, which is connected to electricity and is warm day and night, so that the police standing there will not suffer from frozen hands and feet.

▲ The Big Ben in the Westminster clock tower in London is one of the most famous clocks in the world. It had cracks when it was first hung in 1858. Otherwise, the sound of the timekeeping could reach 20 miles away.

▲ The Bank of England is the national bank of the United Kingdom. All banknote paper is manufactured exclusively in a paper mill in Hampshire. Workers are not allowed to enter other factories except where they work to avoid malpractice.

▲ In Cincinnati, USA, there are four sisters, all of whom are twins. The children born after they got married are also twins. What is particularly interesting is that two of the sisters each have two pairs of twin children.

▲ Canada is also a rich area in the world. Gold mines are often discovered. There was a place that was a thousand miles long, just like a very long gold belt.

Return of the Fisheries Association 180

—Ms. Ye Hua

The ocean and lakes are vast and unpredictable, and scaled creatures thrive, and the benefits are immeasurable. Our country's Mi Xi taught the farming and fishing with nets and mesh. The invention of fishing dates back to ancient times. However, the ignorant fishermen are limited by knowledge and are clumsy in technology. The fishing method is passed down from father to son and has not been changed for many years. The fishing gear is new in belief and old in system, and will never be changed. The entrepreneurial spirit is weak, and they are vagrant on the water, aiming for a full meal. They sit and watch their livelihood decline day by day, and strong neighbors take advantage of the opportunity to hunt us. Wheeled boats are like weaving, and the fishing industry is not repaired, which affects the sea border gate. Thinking about this danger and hidden worries, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mining, the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, and the members of the provincial and municipal party departments have established a fisheries improvement association in view of this. In order to expand the movement, it was decided to hold a fisheries improvement publicity meeting at the Minli Middle School in Shanghai from the 4th to the 10th of this month. Now record one or two to share with readers.

▲The area of Chinese fishing grounds and the ability to fish The association's statistical report stated that the total area of fishing grounds in the world is 1,679,052 square nautical miles, while China's is 271,805 square nautical miles, ranking first in the world. Foreigners estimate that the ocean in our country can produce 466,206,000 yuan, but the current fishing ability is less than one-tenth. At present, the amount of fish caught in our country is only 200,800,000 yuan, of which less than one-quarter are caught by Chinese people themselves, and the rest are owned by the Japanese. How can we not feel heartache.

▲Comparison of the catches of Chinese and Japanese fishermen in Dalian Bay A certain guest who was invited claimed that there are only a hundred Japanese fishermen in Dalian, and ten times as many Chinese, but their income is less than one-tenth of that of the Japanese. Looking at the comparison of the catches of Chinese and Japanese fishermen in November last year, the quantity caught by China was 300,440 catties, and the amount was 22,706 yuan. The quantity caught by Japan was 2,754,694 catties, and the amount was 139,419 yuan. The Japanese residing in Dalian often said proudly, "Chinese fishing grounds need their development." May our people think about it and think about it again. ▲Various sea fish and the import of foreign aquatic products In recent years, European and American fishing ports have been lined up. There are many yellow croakers and silk fish in the East China Sea, small yellow croakers are produced between the East China Sea and the Yellow Sea and in the Bohai Bay. The Yellow Sea produces hairtail, pomfret, and beltfish. The South China Sea produces large beltfish and pomfret. According to President Sun Yat-sen's plan, fish farms and fishing ports should be opened on each coast. This inexhaustible treasure house is enough to enrich people's livelihood and enrich the national economy. The plan has not yet been realized, and the benefits of nets and snares are controlled by foreigners. The total number of aquatic products imported in the 18th year reached 2,688,659 dan, and the total amount was 27,525,828 taels of Guanting silver. This economic loss cannot be said to be insignificant.

▲Green Turtle and Red Turtle, Two-Headed Turtle, as Big as a Boat The exhibition hall has a total of ten. There are many marine meteorological and navigational materials, fishing gear, and fishing tackle on display, as well as new-style fishing boat drawings and nets and aquatic product manufactures from various countries. Looking at all the rooms, the model of our country's fishing grounds, the qiantian mirror, the astronomical clock, and the national emblem made of shells are particularly rare. The green turtle and the red turtle, which are as big as boats, can be called wonders. There is also a yellow croaker that weighs about 40 catties and is more than a zhang long. It is said that only one or two can be obtained in ten years. Its maw is worth a hundred gold, and it is considered a top-grade tonic.

▲Opportunity to Get Fish for Free Everyone Has a Chance This time, 20,000 admission tickets were distributed. 3,000 tickets have gifts. After the guests finished their visits, they held their tickets to the gift area for a lottery. Cuttlefish, squid, small yellow croaker, and prawns are all available. It all depends on luck. I and Zhang Yanggao and Wang Dechang saw that more than 30 people from a certain school only got two small yellow croakers, and the rest were all blank tickets. Zhang Xin, the registration director of Minli Middle School, won a pomfret and a shark with five tickets, which made the viewers envious.

The Variety of Peach Blossoms 181

—Yang Yixiao

▲Peach Blossom Salt Produced in Qin Lake Pond, this salt is the color of peach blossoms and expands and shrinks with the size of the moon.

▲Peach Blossom Vinegar There is a kind of peach blossom vinegar that was valued by the customs of the Tang Dynasty. If you use a little bit of it in vinegar-braised yellow croaker, sweet and sour crucian carp, etc., its taste is more delicious than Zhenjiang vinegar.

▲Peach Blossom Rice Peach Blossom Mountain in Songjiang produces peach blossom rice. Each grain is peach-red in color. When cooked in a wok, it becomes rice. When eaten hot, it is soft, glutinous, fragrant, and beautiful, with a unique flavor.

▲Peach Blossom Powder In women's fragrance powder, mix evenly with rouge, called peach blossom powder. Pour it into the palm of your hand and apply it thinly to your cheeks, and it will be as beautiful as flying rosy clouds.

An Unprecedented Kite Lawsuit 182

—Huang Yingdai

In this delightful spring weather, Shanghai is full of houses, and it is often difficult to find a place to fly a kite. It is better to be in the countryside, where fields and meadows are suitable everywhere. Therefore, the children of Shanghai see the demolition and reconstruction places as good places to fly kites. In their spare time after class, they hold various kites and fly them into the wind. The five colors are reflected in the golden sunlight, creating a unique spectacle. However, if you are not careful, the kite will turn over, and the electric wires on the electric poles will have no mercy, and they will inevitably smash the kite to pieces. This is the inconvenience of flying kites in Shanghai. There is an open space near our school, which is also a place for demolition and reconstruction. On warm and sunny days, there must be countless children in the field competing to fly kites. This reminds me of a kite lawsuit that occurred in Hong Kong last year. The situation is quite laughable. There are many Chinese in Hong Kong. Every spring, there are many children who fly kites. However, after Hong Kong was ceded to the British, all municipal powers were in the hands of the British. The authorities sometimes interfered with children's play. Last year, a child in Hong Kong was detained by the authorities for flying a kite. There was also a lawyer who appeared in court to discuss the matter. It is almost unprecedented for a lawyer to handle a kite flying case. The court said that when the child was flying a kite on Robinson Road, he damaged the telegraph wires and the glass windows of a certain surname, which was illegal. It is stated in the law that the authorities have the right to prohibit any recreational activity that obstructs residents or pedestrians. However, the defendant's lawyer requested proof that flying a kite was listed as a recreational activity, and asked the court who was injured this time and what was damaged. The judge said that no one was injured, but in any case, touching the power line while flying a kite was illegal. The lawyer then asked on what basis this law was based, and asked to check it in court. The judge turned over the law book and found that there was no such law. Therefore, a kite lawsuit finally declared the defendant not guilty.

Method of Artificially Creating Goldfish 183

—Wu Jiren

I am obsessed with goldfish. When I worked for the Star Film Company on Route Doumer last year, my colleagues in the documentation department once promoted me to the title of Goldfish Doctor. I dare not live up to the kindness of those who love me. Therefore, I widely consulted and collected materials on fish farming for the adoption of general hobbyists.

One night, Mr. Wang Xianzai and I visited Mr. Guo Yu, the film manager of the three northeastern provinces, on the fourth floor of the Central Building. Mr. Yu is from Shandong. I immediately inquired about the art of raising fish. Goldfish in our country grow in Shandong Province, and the production in Jinning and Jinan counties is the largest. This is what I have personally experienced and witnessed. Mr. Yu is a learned man, and his words are true. Mr. Yu said, "You only know that goldfish are oviparous, but you don't know that they can also be planted artificially." I was very surprised. Mr. Yu said that the origin of goldfish is comparable to that of flies. They can be both oviparous and wet-born. Oviparous means hatching eggs. Artificial breeding is very peculiar. The method is to put silkworm seeds into the water. The water does not need to be large. A pond of ten feet is enough. There is mud at the bottom of the pond. Put the silkworm seeds in it and let them be exposed to the sun. Let it be even if there are consecutive overcast and rainy days. Once the dog days are over, schools of fish swim at the bottom of the water. Feed them with water fleas every day, and they will grow up. Mr. Yu also said that if you want the goldfish to be red, take yellow silkworm seeds and plant them. If you want them to be white, plant white seeds. If you want them to be red and white, take flower silkworm seeds and do the same. At first, I did not believe it. Then Yu quoted the passage in the Book of Rites (Monthly Orders) "In this month, rotten grass turns into fireflies." I suddenly realized. There is still the art of fish farming, which is not convenient to occupy much space in the free section. It has been published in the "New Family" monthly magazine.

Occasional Talk on Seasonal Objects (II) 184

—Tian Xuwo Sheng

The setting of kites is to make children look up to get rid of internal heat, and also to cure diseases. During the year, when the climate changes, the qi and blood in the human body also undergo major changes, so the elderly often develop old diseases during the two solstices and the four beginnings of the seasons. Children are physically weak, just like the elderly who are weak, so during the festival, there must be one or two medicines to prevent seasonal diseases, which are used in food, but they are all ignorant and do not realize it. The wheat seedlings of Qingming are one example, which are used to get rid of internal heat, and their effect is the same as that of kites. In palaces, the ceilings are often extremely elaborately painted, which also allows the body, which is suffering from ten thousand kinds of worries, to often look up and sigh to get rid of the heat in the five internal organs. Setting up lanterns on the Yuan Night, which is after the beginning of spring, also makes everyone look up and watch to get rid of their internal heat. The intention is very subtle. However, we are buried in our heads all year round, which is inevitably too unsanitary.

Inserting willow branches on Qingming, the custom says to cut the soul to give it. I don't think so. Western oars use willow wine to treat heatstroke and detoxify the blood extremely effectively. Salicylic acid is extracted from the tender skin of willow branches, also known as salicylic acid. After the Qingming Festival, the willows will bloom, and the soft branches will become old. The nutrients contained in them will disappear, so they are cut off before Qingming and inserted outside the door, so that pedestrians and travelers can take them. The intention is also to treat smallpox and chickenpox. If a person suffers from smallpox, suddenly relapses, and cannot break out, then the heat and toxins will sink into the body, and the person will surely die. If you wash it with a decoction of water willow, the pox will immediately reappear, red and full. The heat and toxins are discharged from the pores, and no one will die. If you take this decoction when smallpox is prevalent, it will clear heat and detoxify, and can promote urination, guiding the heat downward, and it is especially effective for treating dysentery. However, it is effective to take a decoction of willow leaves inserted on Qingming Festival, so I think this kind of equipment is just like inserting calamus and mugwort on the door on the Dragon Boat Festival, so that pedestrians suffering from heatstroke and heat rash can use it. Children use willow branches from Qingming to make circles and put them on their necks, in order to prevent throat rash, scrofula, carbuncles, and other diseases. The head is the head of all yang, and the neck is the meridian through which hundreds of meridians pass. It also takes the ability of salicylic acid to detoxify the blood and make it enter from the pores. Putting a willow circle on a dog's neck is to prevent rabid dogs and mad dogs.

Travel Notes in India (XVIII) 185

—Ling Hua

The sport of Indian non-cooperation with Britain has suffered a major blow recently. All British goods are not used. Other countries are also affected. However, in the Orient, Japanese goods are selling well. In terms of customs, it used to be able to collect 1.3 to 1.5 million in taxes per day, but now it has been reduced to 300,000 to 500,000. 1 million a day is gone, and the blow is known. Now large cities can still collect house donations. Tax resistance in the countryside is very common and not easy to collect. An Indian carpenter told me that his factory used to have 150 workers, but now it only has 10. The decline of commerce is known. Most of the Indians hired by the British to be soldiers belong to the Nepalese. Seventy to eighty percent are Nepalese. It is difficult to know the total number accurately. Some say that 400,000 to 500,000 Nepalese are strong. The British hire them to be soldiers, so the British cannot use force to control Nepal. Nepal has helped Britain in the European War with bravery. It cannot be underestimated in Europe. Now Nepal is the only one who is blocking the British from entering Tibet. As for the small country of Bhutan, it is also a Buddhist country, but it has been under British protection for a long time. Daojie Dharma Master said that the Buddhist statues in Bhutan are very beautiful. Now these are the only two Buddhist countries in the north, and only one Ceylon Island in the south.

There will be a problem in India in the future, which is in Erji. The northwest border of India is full of Muslim countries. The reason why they cannot fully help the Indians now is that countries such as Afghanistan are still kingdoms and still have sympathy for Britain. However, their people are quite connected with and help the Indian people. One big problem is that Turkey's railway will be extended to the Persian region. This railway is for those coming from Constantinople, and its funds are provided by Turkey, Germany, and Russia. If the northern route is open, the forces of Russia, Germany, and Turkey can be united. Persia is close to Mumbai in western India. After Turkey changed to a republic, its national power has also become stronger and cannot be insulted.

On the 5th, the Eastern Culture Association was held in the University President's Office. The League or Oriental Culture was proposed by the President, Ruthkrishna, and Professor Barili, a Chinese scholar. 20 professors from other universities initiated it. Among the founders were Persians who were very interested in Eastern culture and wanted to invite me to Tagore University. This association was initially called the Asian Culture League. Because I had the "New Organization" advocacy of the Eastern Renaissance Society, I advocated merging. Asia is not as obscure as the word "Eastern." Everyone agreed with my suggestion to use "Eastern." It will be published in newspapers in the future, and people will be sent to China to connect and exchange knowledge. But I asked what the meaning of Eastern culture is and what the goal should be in order to have value. I said that today is a materialistic world. Those who advocate materialism are Marxists. If they advocate new learning, it is no longer a problem and will inevitably be eliminated. As I advocate, I advocate vitalism. Vitalism is so important that no matter what, it can still stand against the Marxist materialism, because materialism cannot be considered complete. I think the goal of Eastern culture is better built on life. The reason is that it is superior and long. The Indian monk, Shina, also agreed with my argument. Only then can we avoid the criticism of metaphysics. As for how to connect, exchanging knowledge between countries is the first step.

Yarn and Cotton Trends Differ in Spot and Futures Markets 192

The yarn market is calm. The actual market demand is extremely smooth. The purchases in South China and North China are the most diligent. Therefore, the situation of spot yarn is becoming increasingly tight. Most of the Japanese yarn is out of stock, and some brands of local yarn are also out of stock. The export of domestic cotton cloth is still strong. Therefore, a major firm has a calm attitude, but some retailers are still selling short because the overseas yarn and cotton situation is consistently falling. Therefore, although spot sales are enthusiastic, the market price has not risen. If actual sales can continue uninterrupted, the future still has the potential to prosper.

Grain and Rice Market Tight and Continues Firm 195

Zhabei. Yesterday, the number of ships arriving on the road was still scarce. Sales in this street were extremely weak. The top special japonica rice was still priced at 12 yuan 67 jiao, and the transactions were few. Ordinary japonica rice had increased by nearly one jiao in the early morning, but by noon it showed a flat trend, which was due to poor sales. The sales of thin rice were even more sluggish, and the price felt slightly trimmed. The market situation was very sluggish. The demand for Yang Du Xian Bu Xian was flat. The source was not strong, and the market showed a slightly firm trend. The overall market was not much up or down from the previous day. Bai Yuan arrived and sold to the south, and the situation was still good. The lifting households were quite welcome, so the market for special high-quality goods was slightly tight.

Hunan. Yesterday, there were not many ships arriving on the road. The sales in the market were uneven. Changxi, Su Tong, and various machine japonica rice increased due to the active intention of retail and shop parties. The price rose by jiao outside, and the situation began to be stable at the end. The street sales of Nanbang thin early rice were flat, and the price only increased by nearly a foot. The arrival of Yang Du Jian deposits was silent. The board surface had no changes due to the quiet transaction. Various parties' buying of Yin Yuan was still good. Although people's hearts were not good, the cargo owners were extremely anxious to sell, so the market rose by nearly one jiao.

Biao Flour Rises Unanimously 196

Manufacturers' Replenishment in the Near Term... The Rise is Stronger

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market, the prices of each month rose one after another. In the near term, manufacturers replenished their positions, and the rise was even stronger. In the distant term, retail shorts initially followed the replenishment and saw good results, but later they were sold off by inland gangs and became tired again. However, once the manufacturers replenished, people's hearts have turned good. Outside short-sellers did not dare to get involved, and even the short-sellers close to the factory mostly turned long. Therefore, the results were uniformly good in both near and distant terms, calculated as 1.5 points for this month, 1.75 points for next month, 0.75 points for June, 0.25 points for July, 0.5 points for August, and 0.75 points for September.

Wheat Market Near Term Firm, Distant Term Tired 197

Yesterday's wheat market, near term months tended to be firm and rise, distant term months rose and fell again. The market was near term firm and distant term tired. In the near term, due to the active sales of the current flour of the manufacturers, many foreign wheat hedges were proposed. The distant term was caused by inland customers selling off. At the closing price, the current month was up by 3 points, the next month was up by 1 point, June was down by 2 points, September was down by 2 points, July was down by 1 point, August was unchanged, and the arrival and sale of the current wheat were both lacking. Foreign wheat was scheduled to arrive and there was none. Overseas telegrams reported an increase the day before, but yesterday they reported a small 3 jiao or so.

Ke Xian Guangdong Sales Slightly Move 198

Yesterday's Ke Xian market situation was still lively. Because the market price had fallen behind some time ago, it aroused the trial handling of this street and Guangdong gang. The Guangdong gang's trial sales were still worthwhile, and there were inquiries every day. In addition to loading more than 1,000 bags before, they also purchased 400 or 500 bags of Jiangxi rice in the market. This street also followed up and purchased. Therefore, although the market price did not rise, the market atmosphere was not as stagnant as it was a few days ago. A total of more than 100 bags of early Jiangxi machine rice were transacted in the market, priced at 10 yuan 06 jiao half to 10 yuan 06 jiao, and more than 1,000 bags of late machine rice, priced at 11 yuan 3 jiao half to 11 yuan, were divided up by this street and the Guangdong gang. However, because the Guangdong gang had not yet cleared the stocks they had handled some time ago, they only went to a small number yesterday.

Period Bean Near Term Tired, Distant Term Stable 199

Yesterday, the opening of the yellow bean market in the morning was quite firm, because the customers of each gang were still very diligent in their intentions to enter the market. The period price of each month was not much up or down compared to the previous suspension. Until the opening in the afternoon, the market tended to be tired because the connected news was slightly weak and many long positions in this month were sold out. It was also heard that the gold market reported small in the afternoon and people's hearts were pessimistic. However, because there were inquiries from the inland gang, the distant term was able to stabilize. At the close, April was 4 taels 6 qian 3, down by 2 points, and May was 4 taels 6 qian 1, and the market was stable.

Sugar Market Raw and White Sugar Increase by Half a Cent 200

Yesterday, sugar market reports from producing areas stated that Cuban raw sugar prices remained stable. New York futures for all months rose by one cent, except for December, which rose by two cents. Java spot prices also showed little fluctuation in the near term, with June rising by 0.125. At the association's market, the demand for Dutch sugar No. 24 was strong, with transaction prices reaching taels 10.05. High-quality sugar reached taels 10.055, and medium white sugar taels 9.9, with brisk trading. The company offered 1,000 bags of spot medium white sugar from Huaxin at taels 9.9, maintaining a firm market. The Japanese sugar market also saw gradual increases, with frequent transactions: N mark at taels 10.035, J mark at taels 10.07, YP mark at taels 10.055 to 10.06, YRO at taels 9.8 to 9.825, SH mark at taels 9.95. The overall trend remained firm and strong, with no signs of optimism.

Silk and Tea Factories Actively Selling Dried Silk to the United States 201

Yesterday, the local foreign silk market continued to be strong. It was observed that American firms in Shanghai, noting the thin inventories at silk factories and the relatively low prices, seized the opportunity to act. There was also a transfer of high-grade white dried silk for the U.S. market to Shanghai. Yesterday, Wei Cheng and others imported 140 bales of white factory silk and 100 bales of white dried silk to Shanghai, with firm prices reported.

Overseas Silk Waste Standard Continues to Rise 202

In recent years, the sales of semi-silk fabrics in Europe and the United States have been brisk, leading to a surge in demand for silk waste and rising market prices. Last week, the asking price for silk waste standards in the Marseille market continued to rise, with white silk waste increasing by 3.75 pence per kilogram and yellow silk waste by 1.25 pence.

Foreign Tea Market Turns Quiet 203

Yesterday, the local foreign tea market turned quiet. There were no transactions for needle tea, eyebrow tea, or pearl tea. The entire market saw only Jardine Matheson & Co. purchasing 129 chests of Luzhuang Zhenmei tea, priced at taels 48, with no increase or decrease compared to the previous period. Currently, there are still more than 15,000 chests in stock on the market, making it difficult to clear them in the near future.

Piece Goods, Eastern Goods, Woolens Revival in Sales 204

Recently, Eastern goods, woolens, and serge have seen renewed activity, with a surge in sales, mostly purchased by Japanese firms such as Mitsui and Iwai. Currently, ordinary blue-gray serge, mixed-color twill, chocolate twill, and white serge, Pi Qu, etc., are all selling well. High-quality serge is priced at taels 3.23, ordinary serge at taels 2.89, and chocolate twill at taels 4.34. It is reported that orders are being placed for ordinary Melton, fine wool, and facing cloth for the second half of the year, totaling fifty to sixty pieces.

Youth Corner Submission Guidelines 206

(1) Articles should focus on discussions about youth issues, news about domestic and foreign schools and students, essays, descriptions of school life, and personal writings. The style is not limited.

(2) Illustrations should be limited to those related to youth issues.

(3) Photographs that qualify include those related to youth life (such as sports, travel, visits, theater performances, lectures, gatherings, exhibitions, various competitions, etc.), school news, and youth movements. Both individual and group photos are welcome.

(4) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(5) The number of words per article should not exceed 2,000.

(6) Do not write manuscripts horizontally. Do not use cursive writing. Western text should be omitted where possible. If it is absolutely necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

(7) Do not use blue ink to draw illustrations, and do not use colored paper. Use white paper and black ink.

(8) Please specify "Youth Corner Editorial Department" as the recipient of the submissions.

(9) All submissions, whether published or not, will not be returned. If a return is required, it should be stated in advance.

(10) Remuneration for articles is divided into three categories: 3 yuan, 2 yuan, and 1 yuan per thousand words. Illustrations and photographs are subject to the same rates. Remuneration for special contributions will be calculated separately.

Shanghai Market

Market News 207

▲The Joint Reserve Depository announces that it is jointly established by the Yien Yieh Commercial Bank, the Kin Cheng Banking Corporation, the Chung Nan Bank, and the Continental Bank to handle the issuance of Chung Nan Bank notes. According to the depository's issuance regulations, the issuance of banknotes is fully backed, with a minimum of 60% in cash reserves and a maximum of 40% in guarantee reserves. Weekly announcements are made, and the records are audited by the four banks' auditors and accountants. The 66th announcement of the Shanghai Reserve Depository on April 4, 1931, is as follows: circulating notes totaled $35,511,6352; total reserves amounted to $35,511,6352, including cash reserves of $21,199,1300.42 and guarantee reserves of $13,125,051.58.

▲The Palace Hotel declares that its facilities are magnificent, its location is bustling yet quiet, and it is a social center for Shanghai's high society. In addition to the existing tea dances, a mini-golf course has been set up on the first floor and is now fully open.

▲The Chung Mei Lun Silk and Satin Store on East Gate Road, Nanshi, announces that it has been one week since its opening. Therefore, it plans to hold a one-month anniversary grand sale on the 10th of this month. At the same time, the Mei Ya Silk Factory will sell its remaining clothing materials at a discounted cost and will provide silk scarves and Mei Ya silk cheongsam materials as gifts to thank customers for their patronage.

▲The Mao Chang Optical Company, located at the old warehouse street entrance on the west side of the Old North Gate, declares that it was established the earliest and is the pioneer of the optical industry in Shanghai. With strong capital and a large scale, it has separate retail, wholesale, manufacturing, and inspection departments. All types of glasses produced are novel, unique, beautiful, and durable, and have long been sold throughout the country. Recently, to facilitate out-of-town customers, a special mail-order department has been established. For all mail orders, there is no need to remit payment in advance; payment can be made upon delivery. Therefore, it is welcomed by domestic and foreign counterparts and general customers.

▲The Wan Yuan Xiang Embroidery Shop declares that Xiang embroidery is a unique art product of Hunan, with hundreds of years of history and has long been praised by people at home and abroad. This shop, in order to promote women's industry and promote Chinese art, has hired domestic and foreign masters of calligraphy and painting to guide improvements. A large number of new products have now arrived in Shanghai, including landscapes, figures, flowers, birds, animals, and paintings by Mr. Yu Youren, Mr. Tan Zu'an, and other famous people from ancient and modern times. The workmanship is exquisite, and orders from various provinces and cities have been pouring in, truly a case of supply falling short of demand.

▲The Zhenmin Underwear Company, located at the intersection of Avenue Haig and Wenzhou Road, declares that it purchases Western-style underwear and has recently received a large batch of unique underwear materials with many colors, which cannot be listed in detail. In addition, it has specially hired senior technicians to specialize in making Western-style underwear, with fast and durable products, and guaranteed delivery on time, which has always been appreciated by the community. Wholesale and retail sales are particularly considerate. This announcement is made.

▲The Sincere Company on Nanjing Road declares that its sports department on the second floor has specially hired professional technicians to repair rackets for customers. The highest quality Singapore string is only $2.50 per racket and can be picked up the next day.

▲The Fushou Pharmacy, located at the intersection of Fourth Road and Wangping Street, declares that it has recently received disinfectant perfume from Germany, which is effective in preventing meningitis, scarlet fever, and various epidemics. In recent days, wholesale purchases have been pouring in from near and far. In addition, this shop's original one-corner pharmaceuticals are economical and practical. All are welcome to try them for verification.

Theater News 208

▲The Baixing Grand Theater, located at the intersection of Route Ghisi and Rue Richelieu, declares that since the premiere of the shocking world-unique international blockbuster "National Soul," it has caused a sensation in society and aroused enthusiastic visits from patriotic people. Even Japanese residents in Shanghai with patriotic enthusiasm have come in droves, with every show sold out. This theater is screening it for four consecutive days to make it accessible to a wider audience. Because this film is not allowed to be screened by the authorities in the foreign concessions, there will be no further screening opportunities after it finishes at this theater. It is hoped that the public will not miss this opportunity.

▲The Jiuxing Grand Theater declares that since its recent reorganization, the silent and sound films it has screened have been the best of the time. Today, this theater is screening the First National Company's latest work from last year, the great romantic musical dialogue blockbuster "Autumn Waves of Resentment," starring screen flower Corinne Maya and concert star and violin master James Hall. Ms. Ke uses her enchanting autumn waves and charming performances, singing sweet and moving love songs with her clear and melodious voice, such as "Lover Returns" and "Welcoming Autumn Waves," accompanied by James' violin, making it even more beautiful and exceptionally pleasing to the ear. With comedy, song, and dance, plus the great Irish scenery, it is truly a rare and excellent film.
